Important News 2

Zhang Huizan Appointed Commander-in-Chief for Bandit Suppression

Zhang to Immediately Depart for Jiangxi to Suppress Communists

Jin Handing's Entire Division to Return to Jiangxi to Assist in Suppression

Provincial Government Establishes Four Police Training Regiments

Nanchang dispatch, 18th. Besides the local defense forces in each county, the bandit suppression forces in this province include six brigades under Dai Yue, Zhu Yaohua, Cheng Guangyao, Tang Yunshan, Deng Ying, and Zhang Yuren, as well as two regiments under Chen Lei and Zeng Zhenxiang. The military strength is not weak. However, without a unified commander, the forces are difficult to concentrate, so Zhu Mao's bandits can still flee from one place to another. Chairman Lu therefore submitted a request some days ago, and Commander-in-Chief Chiang appointed Zhang Huizan, the commander of the 18th Division, concurrently as the Bandit Suppression Commander for the entire province of Jiangxi, entrusting him with full responsibility. Zhang telegraphed his acceptance of the position today and established the Bandit Suppression Headquarters for the entire province of Jiangxi. It is divided into four sections: Staff, Adjutant, Secretariat, and Military Law. The Chief of Staff of the division, Staff Officer Xiao, will serve concurrently as the Chief of the General Staff. The Chief of the Garrison Headquarters, Staff Officer Huang, will serve concurrently as the Chief of the Staff Section. The Chief of the Enforcement Office of the division, Xu, will serve concurrently as the Chief of Military Law. Huang Xingyi will be appointed as the Chief of the Secretariat. With the internal organization in place, Zhang plans to lead the headquarters to Ji'an in western Jiangxi tomorrow to command everything. The Provincial Government's Bandit Suppression Propaganda Office will also follow along. However, at a time when bandits and communists are as numerous as hemp and the red flames are high, Commander-in-Chief Zhang is still concerned that the military strength is insufficient. In addition to urging the Luo Lin division and the Yan Zhongru brigade, which have been ordered to Jiangxi for bandit suppression, to set off quickly, he has also telegraphed Chairman Chiang to order Jin Handing's entire division to return to Jiangxi to assist in the suppression. It is said that Commander-in-Chief Chiang has approved Jin's entire division to return to Jiangxi via telegram. Therefore, Division Commander Zhang telegraphed Jin yesterday, saying, "Commander-in-Chief Jin, secret. Your younger brother previously received an order to command the Jiangxi campaign against Zhu Mao's troops. Because the strength was weak, I did not dare to take office rashly. Now I have received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Chiang, asking me to request your honorable division to return to Jiangxi to suppress the Jiangxi bandits. I was overjoyed to hear this. I will immediately rush to the front to supervise the troops. I await your telegram for the plan and will work hard to advance the campaign, hoping to follow in your honorable footsteps to clear the Jiangxi bandits, relieve the Central Government's internal worries, and eliminate the local scourge of many years. I am inspired and eager to serve. I send this sincere message. Your brother, Zhang Huizan, stamped at dawn." As for the Provincial Government, regarding the bandit disaster as the most serious issue at present, it has devoted all its efforts to the suppression work. In addition to drafting a bandit suppression plan and establishing a Bandit Suppression Committee, it has also set a deadline of April 1st to establish four police training regiments to establish self-defense forces to fundamentally eradicate the bandits and communists.

He Chengjun Returns to Hankou by Plane

He Issues Statement to the Press

Hankou dispatch. He Chengjun, Acting Director of the Wuhan Provisional Headquarters, was summoned by Commander-in-Chief Chiang via telegram. He took a commercial airline flight to Nanjing on the 15th of this month, arriving at noon. Regarding the southern section of the Pinghan Railway, the defense of northern Hubei, the pacification of the entire province, and the Wuhan garrison, he separately requested instructions when he met with Commander-in-Chief Chiang. He only returned to Hankou on the original flight at 8:00 AM on the 17th, arriving at the airport at 2:00 PM in the afternoon. Those who came to the airport to welcome him included the Second Army Commander Jiang Dingwen, the Tenth Army Commander Xu Yuanquan, the Thirteenth Army Commander Xia Douyin, and the Chief of Staff of the Fifth Route Army, Chen Guangzu. After He got off the plane, he and Jiang Dingwen and others took separate cars to the Provisional Headquarters for a tea talk meeting. First, He reported on his visit to the Commander-in-Chief in Nanjing and the Commander-in-Chief's future military measures in this area. Then, Jiang Dingwen and others separately reported on the defense situation and requested instructions on everything. It is said that there was also a brief discussion on the current situation. The meeting lasted two hours. He then received the press and issued the following statement, "I was summoned to Nanjing on the 15th and met with the Commander-in-Chief that evening to request instructions on military matters. In order to implement the policy of peaceful unification, the Central Government has been lenient with all reactionary soldiers, hoping they will repent. If they continue to be unrepentant and launch large-scale attacks again, we will launch another major campaign. Now, Yan Xishan is surrounded by reactionaries and is using retreat as a way to advance. His conspiracies are becoming increasingly exposed. If he destroys peaceful unification, he will be digging his own grave. The Central Government has its own methods to eliminate reactionaries when the time comes. As for the rumors that Feng Yuxiang has arrived at Tongguan, this is true. However, Feng's troops were previously defeated by the Central Government, and their elite troops have been exhausted. Moreover, there are great internal divisions, so it is difficult for them to cooperate with Yan. Currently, Henan Province Chairman Han Fuju and Commander-in-Chief Shi Yousan are wholeheartedly supporting the Central Government, and their troops have advanced to the Daokou Zhangde area in Hebei. Even if Yan and Feng want to launch an attack, it is impossible. As for all matters here, I have requested instructions from the Commander-in-Chief on essential points. All the troops in northern Hubei have also been assigned by Commander-in-Chief Chiang to be under the command of Tenth Army Commander Xu Yuanquan. Regarding the pacification issue, the establishment of four Provincial Defense Regiments has been approved, and the guns will be allocated by the Central Government. After the soldiers are recruited, we will submit a request to the Central Government to receive them." (March 18th)

News of the Reorganization of the Jiangsu Provincial Government

There has been talk of reorganizing the Jiangsu Provincial Government for a long time, but it has only been realized recently due to the many changes in the situation. It is said that the members announced by the National Government this time were all carefully considered before a decision was made. However, most of the members are scattered in Nanjing and Shanghai, so the date of their assumption of office has not yet been determined. It was originally decided that Hu Puan, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, would come to Zhenjiang after receiving the appointment letter from the National Government. Now, because of a letter urging from Ye Chucang, he plans to go to Nanjing first. After everything is negotiated, he will come to the province. Sun Hongzhe, the Director of the Department of Construction, plans to come to Zhenjiang before the 20th. As for the three members who are leaving the Provincial Government, Niu Miaozhang, Zhang Shouyong originally served concurrently as the Director of the Jiangsu Department of Finance while serving as the Vice Minister of Finance. From now on, he will be stationed in Nanjing permanently, serving only as the Vice Minister of Finance. It was initially said that Chairman Niu would be reassigned as the Chief of Civil Officials of the National Government, but this has now been proven inaccurate. It is said that the Ministry of Interior will be reorganized, and Niu may be promoted to Minister. Miao Bin went to Nanjing in a hurry the day before yesterday and returned to the province yesterday. He has ordered the staff of the Department of Civil Affairs to rush to handle the handover. It is expected that the affairs of the Department will be handed over completely within a week, and then he will go to Nanjing. According to reports, the authorities intend to give him a military position.

After the reorganization of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, new plans will be made for the command and organization of police affairs. The general situation is that the affairs of water and land public security will be separated from the Department of Civil Affairs and established as an independent agency, with the new Provincial Committee member Li Mingyang responsible for overseeing it. It is said that the National Government previously decided that each province could establish a police department. When Chairman Niu was the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs in the Jiangsu Provincial Government, he also established a Water and Land Public Security Administration Office. It is said that the new Provincial Government's organization of the police department will be directly under the Provincial Government. As for the suppression of lake bandits, the Department of Civil Affairs previously planned to establish a Pacification Office in a suitable location in the Taihu Lake area to be responsible for pacification. It is now planned that after the new members take office, they will discuss with the Zhejiang Provincial Government to establish the Taihu Lake Pacification Office as soon as possible in order to eliminate the lake bandits.

Su Bingwen Succeeds Liang Zhongjia's Position

Russian Troops Still Provoking on the Border

Harbin Dispatch, 14th. On the evening of the 13th, over one hundred Russian cavalrymen secretly entered Tuolannor and looted two steel cannons, over thirty cannonballs, and twenty-six Type 38 rifles from our army. At the time, our army raised their guns to pursue, but were stopped by their superiors, so they were allowed to loot as they pleased. That night at 10:00 PM, thunderous artillery fire occurred between the Xiaozhan train station at the 18th milepost and the main station, lasting for half an hour before stopping. Merchants and residents were startled from their sleep, and many were panicked and did not know what to do. Fortunately, the artillery fire soon stopped, and they calmed down. Now that Liang Zhongjia has passed away in Manzhouli, merchants and residents have lost their security, and many have moved back to the mainland. Although the troops have formed a joint defense and are under martial law, it is not enough to calm people's hearts. As for Liang's vacant position (commander of the 15th Brigade, Pacification Commissioner of Hulunbuir, and commander of the Harbin-Manchuria Railway Protection Army), the province has announced that Su Bingwen, the Chief of Staff of the Border Defense Deputy Commander-in-Chief's Office, will succeed him. He will go to take over the duties within days. Liang's coffin has not yet been transported back to his hometown. In addition to the three thousand yuan allocated by Zhang Xueliang for funeral expenses, Wan Fulin of Heilongjiang also gave two thousand yuan and sent Dou Lianfang, the Director of the Public Security Administration Office, to Hailar to represent him in paying respects.

Zhejiang Construction Department Presents a Report on the Process of Banning Artificial Fertilizers

Lists Seven Suggestions for Banning

Requests the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining to Take Charge

The Zhejiang Construction Department believes that in recent years, artificial fertilizers have flooded the market with varying qualities. Farmers blindly believe in advertisements and do not distinguish between good and bad. They casually purchase and use them, often leading to the deterioration of the soil and damage to crops, which is extremely important for the future of agriculture. Natural fertilizers, such as soybean cakes, rapeseed cakes, and cottonseed cakes, are instead sold abroad at low prices. Previously, they jointly proposed with the Department of Finance to reduce and exempt natural fertilizer taxes and ban exports in order to provide relief. The proposal has been approved and implemented by the Provincial Government Committee. An agricultural chemistry laboratory has also been attached to the Mineral Resources Survey Institute to collect samples of artificial fertilizers for precise chemical testing at any time in order to find ways to ban them. At the same time, a booklet advising farmers to use more natural fertilizers has been printed and distributed to various counties to widely encourage them. Now, they have received an instruction from the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining, stating that the Shanghai Ellis Foreign Firm has submitted a request to instruct the firm's fertilizer powder sold in Zhejiang Province to be slightly promoted. The original submission was copied and ordered to be observed and handled. The situation of Zhejiang Province's promotion of natural fertilizers and banning of artificial fertilizers has been reported to the Ministry of Agriculture, and the following suggestions for banning are listed: (1) Please issue a general order to the agricultural agencies under the Ministry's jurisdiction and across the country to conduct more tests and widely publicize the large quantities of natural fertilizers produced in various places so that farmers will be happy to use them. (2) Please consult with the Ministry of Finance and consult with the provincial and municipal governments to issue a general order to exempt taxes and fees on natural fertilizers produced in their respective areas and prohibit their export in order to avoid sales abroad so that domestic farmers can purchase and use them at low prices. (3) Please consult with the three ministries of Finance, Transportation, and Railways, and the provincial and municipal governments to increase tariff taxes and transportation costs on imported artificial fertilizers in order to restrict them. (4) Please plan to establish a government-business joint-stock fertilizer factory to promote them in practice. (5) Those who manufacture high-quality artificial fertilizers in our country should be clearly defined in regulations and given special awards. (6) The mineral fertilizers produced in various provinces should be consulted with the provincial and municipal governments to find ways to explore and extract them for use in the common manufacture of fertilizers. (7) Please order the agricultural product inspection institutes under the Ministry's jurisdiction to strictly define standards and issue certificates carefully for imported artificial fertilizers. The unqualified fertilizers must be widely announced and strictly prohibited from sale in order to prevent farmers from being deceived.

Local News

Songjiang

Record of a Trial Involving a Litigation Settlement: Shen Anfu, a wealthy man from Yaojiajiao in Xinzhuang Township, passed away on December 26th of last year. Because he had no children during his lifetime, he adopted his sister-in-law's son, Wang Zuoliang, as his son, giving him the surname Shen, and adopted Ou Hong as his daughter. Wang Zuoliang was adopted at the age of six and is now seventeen years old. In December of last year, when Anfu was seriously ill, he invited relatives Liu Jianzhang, Liu Shoujian, Wang Baoxian, and his nephew Shen Jiajun to sign a will, giving 300 mu of land to his nephew Jiajun and the rest to Xu Zuoliang. However, although the will was made at that time, it was not signed by Jiajun. Recently, Jiajun filed a lawsuit against Shen Liu (Anfu's wife) for adopting a different surname and disrupting the family order. The county government held a hearing today. The plaintiff Shen Jiajun hired lawyer Qu Yue as his assistant, and Shen Zuoliang hired lawyer Zhang Enhao as his agent due to illness. Shen Liu personally appeared in court. After the judge Du summoned the plaintiff and defendant to state their cases, the plaintiff did not recognize the will, saying that it was fundamentally illegal and could not take effect. The defendant presented Liu Shoujian and Wang Baoxian as witnesses, proving that Jiajun was indeed present when the will was made. Then, Zhang Enhao stated that the plaintiff's lawsuit for adopting a child required the consent of both parties. Now, the person being inherited does not want the plaintiff to be the heir, which has been proven in the will. Therefore, whether there is a dispute over the right to sue in this case is still a question. The plaintiff's assistant, Qu Yue, stated that according to our country's customs, a fox dies with its head facing its hill. After Anfu died, the plaintiff did hold the head during the encoffining, which is not difficult to investigate. The judge, seeing that both parties were wealthy, tried to mediate, instructing them to mediate within twenty days. Both lawyers were very supportive, and the court adjourned.

Water Police Squad Captures Kidnappers: He Yalin, the captain of the first squad of the water police squad, recently captured a kidnapper named He Jiulin in Xiangqiao and rescued Yang Yunqing from Qingliang Nunnery, Zhang Lin from Shisi Jing, Cao Gengyun from Chenmu, and Gu Zhenlin and Feng Tang's Feng Yanghua from Feng Tang area near Daliudang. Wuxi

Rogue Soldiers Kill Villagers While Robbing Gambling: Jinghui Temple, located in the 326th Tu of Xin'an Township, is one of the eight major temples in Wuyi. Incense is very popular. Every year on the nineteenth day of the second month of the lunar calendar, it is the birthday of Guanyin. The temple holds a warm-up ceremony the day before, chanting incense and chanting scriptures all night. The day before yesterday was the day of the warm-up ceremony, so the temple was extremely lively. Some villagers took the opportunity to open a gambling den near the temple at the Zhou Shen family's house, shouting and drinking, and the winnings and losses were quite large. Unexpectedly, at about 11:00 PM, more than ten rogue soldiers suddenly came, holding long guns, and crowded into the Zhou Shen family's house. The gamblers fled in panic. The rogue soldiers opened fire and fired into the crowd. At that time, a villager named Xu Aquan, nicknamed "Puluotou" Aquan, was fat and unable to run away, so he was shot in the abdomen and fell to the mulberry field outside the wall, dying instantly. Another villager, Yuan Aquan, was shot in the left leg, and blood flowed like a torrent, kicking the ground in extreme pain. The rogue soldiers, seeing that they had caused trouble, left swaggeringly. Afterwards, the injured Yuan Aquan was sent to the Western doctor at Hua Dafang Zhuang for treatment. It is said that the injury was quite serious and may become a disability. Yesterday, Zhou Puzhai, the deputy head of Jinghui Township, and Xu Asan, the younger brother of the deceased Xu Aquan, came to the city to report to the county for an inquest. This morning, Judge Yu took a steamboat to the countryside for an inquest.

The Exhibition of Local Products from Eight Counties and Cities is Scheduled to be Held: The exhibition of local products from eight counties and cities initiated by County Magistrate Sun of this county has been decided to be held for the first time at Huishan Town in Wuxi on April 20th. It is learned that the silk exhibition of the Nanjing National Goods Commercial Field and the national product exhibition of the provincial capital will both be held on April 15th, at the same time as the exhibition of eight counties and cities, which will have an impact on the collection of products from various counties. Moreover, counties such as Yixing and Liyang have sent letters requesting a postponement of the exhibition period due to the lack of time to collect products. In view of this situation, County Magistrate Sun decided to postpone the exhibition period of the eight counties and cities to September.

Bandits Commit Robbery in Sanjia Village: A ancestral hall house of the Bu Qian family in Sanjia Village, Hongshengli, Nanyan City, was guarded by Shen Er. On the evening of the day before yesterday, four or five bandits suddenly came, holding weapons such as pistols, iron rulers, and electric batons, and entered over the wall. They opened Shen's daughter's door, tied up Shen's daughter and Er's young son with ropes, and beat them severely, causing Shen's daughter to be covered in wounds. The bandits then ransacked the boxes and chests at will, searching and looting. After an hour, they left with the stolen goods. After checking, it was reported that they stole twelve yuan in silver dollars, four jiao in small silver dollars, four thousand copper coins, over two shi of white rice, and clothing, jewelry, etc., totaling a loss of over one hundred yuan.

New Organization of the Municipal Government: Since the establishment of the Wuxi Municipal Government Preparatory Office in the autumn of last year, it has been six months. The Municipal Government Preparatory Office received a decree from the Department of Civil Affairs issuing the organizational method of the Municipal Government Committee, requiring the original Municipal Government Preparatory Office to be abolished immediately. The Wuxi Municipal Government Committee should be reorganized, following the precedents of the Construction Committee of the National Government and the Construction Committee of the Jiangsu Provincial Capital. The organization of the committee stipulates that there should be seven to eleven members, with the county magistrate as an ex officio member and concurrently the chairman of the committee. The remaining members should be appointed from local people with prestige and experience in municipal administration. The Municipal Government Preparatory Office is currently actively preparing for reorganization.

The Public Security Bureau Transfers the Chief of the Dong Sub-Bureau: Li Leng, the director of the Wuyi County Public Security Bureau, in order to implement the internal and external duties handled by police officers of the same rank, has transferred Yu Baoying, the chief of inspectors of the bureau, to serve as the chief of the sixth sub-bureau. Changshu

The Western Doctor's Autopsy of the Liu Daughter-in-Law Case: After the autopsy of Cai Lianbao, the daughter-in-law of the Liu family in Shanxiang Lane, Dr. Gu Yuanhao of Jishan Hospital disagreed with the other nine doctors because he had not co-signed the report. The nine doctors had sent a letter to Dr. Gu requesting a response. Before receiving the letter, Dr. Gu responded to several points based on newspaper reports as follows: (1) Whether the section of the intestine removed was indeed the duodenum was uncertain as he had not examined it and thus could not say for sure. For the sake of caution, a re-examination was necessary. If, as Dr. Zhou stated, the section removed was part of the jejunum, about three inches from the stomach, then he believes that there was no need to leave these three inches, causing the important parts (the openings of the bile and pancreatic ducts) to be left in the abdominal cavity, while removing a more distant and difficult segment. (2) Methods of death by poisoning include arsenic, phosphorus, mercury, and acid, all of which are effective. Since the gentlemen suspected opium poisoning, was the testing and determination recorded in the examination report? (3) Before any autopsy, one must determine what illness caused the death of the deceased. Only if no signs of death are found can one suspect poison. During the autopsy, one should be thorough in every aspect, such as examining the brain, large and small intestines, gallbladder, bile ducts, reproductive organs, etc. During the county government meeting, he stated that the brain should be dissected, but the gentlemen said it was not important and cancelled the idea. If important parts can be cancelled, then there seems to be no possibility of further suggestions. (4) There are regulations for dissecting corpses. He originally wanted to state at the scene, but Dr. Zhou suddenly split the middle of the abdominal cavity. If a correction was to be made, there were many doctors involved, which was awkward. Unexpectedly, a sincere effort turned into an opinion, which is deeply regrettable. In short, we cannot shirk responsibility for the negligence of this autopsy. After the publication of this article, Chen Shitao, the trial officer of the county government, convened nine doctors who had dissected and chemically examined Cai's corpse, including Zhou Mansun, Gu Jianshan, Shao Yufan, Xue Baoshan, Xie Tang, Gu Zhiru, Wu Juncheng, Zhou Tianlai, and Zhou Guanwen, along with Huang Chengxi, the president of Jishan Hospital, and Dr. Gu Yuanhao, at 4:00 PM on the 15th to discuss the autopsy. The meeting was chaired by Chen Shitao. On that day, Gu Jianshan, Zhou Mansheng, Shao Yufan, and Gu Yuanhao engaged in a major debate. The Qin Bao reporter also testified that Gu Yuanhao did say he had cultivated cerebrospinal fluid after the autopsy. Therefore, this newspaper reported the facts. The chairman said to Gu that since he had denied it, the newspaper should be asked to correct it. The Qin Bao reporter said that Dr. Gu did say this and it was not convenient to correct it. The chairman then said that the reporters from each newspaper could publish the discussions at the meeting and then adjourned the meeting. The day after the meeting, Huang Chengxi, the president of Jishan Hospital, raised the issue of the dissection instruments. All the knives, pliers, and instruments used to dissect Cai's corpse were newly purchased by Jishan Hospital. Gu Yuanhao brought these instruments to the autopsy site and Zhou Mansun performed the abdominal procedure. Afterwards, it was discovered that these instruments were contaminated with cadaveric poison and could no longer be used for dissecting live people. Sterilization requires 120 pounds of firepower, but the hospital's sterilizer only has 100 pounds of firepower. Therefore, these instruments are now useless except for dissecting corpses. Fortunately, only a portion of the instruments were used in this case. If all were used, the value would be around a thousand gold. It is heard that President Huang will inquire with Gu Yuanhao whether he mentioned the disposal of the instruments during the autopsy before deciding on a solution.

Scheduled Demolition of the Outer Walls of the Big and Small East Gates: The Construction Bureau presented a request to the Construction Department to use the bricks and stones from the demolition of the outer walls of the Big and Small East Gates to build bridges and culverts on the Xichang section of the Yichang Road. Jiangyin

The Finance Bureau's Debt is Difficult for the County Magistrate to Approve: The Finance Bureau, due to the dire financial situation of the locality, drafted relief measures, first raising a short-term loan of 40,000 yuan, and then soliciting local public bonds of 100,000 yuan, submitting them to the county for approval. Yesterday, an instruction was received stating that the local expenses not collected under the busy transport item in previous years amounted to more than 150,000 yuan. The reason for the difficulty in the expenses of various agencies is not that there is no money to collect, but that there is money that is not collected. The bureau's responsibility lies in not devising ways to collect and promote prosperity, but in advocating ways to borrow money. Regardless of the large number of bonds, the people find it difficult to bear, and they ignore the money that should be collected, and willingly borrow with heavy interest, causing losses to the locality, which is also contrary to reason. It was found that at the 49th county political meeting on January 6, a resolution was made regarding the problem of insufficient income and expenditure of various agencies, and the bureau was asked to formulate a method and convene various agencies that use money to discuss it together. The bureau shirks its responsibility, which is not appropriate. The example of raising money in the locality when military affairs occur is used in the submission, but there is no indication of money in the budget. It is a fallacy to cite the previous example, cutting flesh to mend sores. If this continues, the locality will inevitably have more than 100,000 yuan of debt forever, which is difficult to approve.

Construction Bureau Officials Beaten: Regarding the case of officials of the Jiangdu Construction Bureau being beaten by road workers, it was recently heard that County Magistrate Chen plans to go to the countryside tomorrow to conduct an on-site investigation of everything, and plans to convene the general and sub-section chiefs of each section of the Yanghuo Road to instruct the workers to start work immediately. Brothers Fighting Over Wife Leads to Cracking of Robbery Case: In Fanchuan Town, which borders the county and Gaoyou Tai County, there is a watchman, Chen Longzi. Half a year ago, a mother and daughter from Yancheng avoiding famine had nowhere to rely, and they begged from door to door during the day and stayed at Chen Longzi's house at night. Over time, Chen fell in love with the daughter of a refugee (18 years old). This spring, the mother wanted to take her daughter back to Yancheng, and Longzi agreed. Later, the girl's mother found out and demanded a lot of money. So Longzi made an appointment for ten days and agreed to find a way to marry her. Unexpectedly, after Longzi left, his daughter had an affair with Longzi's brother. When Longzi returned with the money, his lover was already owned by his brother. Longzi was furious, but Longzi not only refused to give in, but also sued the local merchants' association because his younger brother's money came from an unknown source. When Longzi heard the news, he disappeared. Later, Chen Mapi, who was an accomplice of Longzi in doing evil outside, was arrested and confessed that in the past six months, he had robbed Da Da Tong Yang Xiaolun and wealthy families in Taizhou Gaoyou, with more than 20 accomplices. The day before yesterday, Chen and Longzi robbed a family in Ximen, Tai County, and Chen Longzi divided more than 100 yuan to use for marrying a wife. In Chen Mapi's house, a pistol was found, along with 100 yuan and several pawn tickets. The water police team used a boat to send the above two people to Tai County. When the boat arrived at Laoyutao, bandit Zhou, was arrested and sent to the county together. Recently, it was heard that more than ten criminals have been arrested in this case. This can also be said to be the broad and inescapable net of heaven.

Qingjiang

Lianshui Plans Long-Distance Buses: Since the Jiangbei Highway Bureau stopped operating long-distance buses from Huaiyin to Lianshui, people in Lianshui felt that transportation was inconvenient and built two long-distance bus routes, Lianguan and Lianhuai. All the roads and bridges on the two routes have been repaired. It is heard that the vehicles were also approved by Gu Zhutong, commander of the Second Army of the Army, who donated two cars due to his relationship with his hometown, one for the south line and one for the north line, both on alternate days. As soon as the vehicles arrive in Lian, they will start business.

Huai'an Middle School Suspends Classes: Wang Zhongqi, principal of Jiangsu Provincial Huai'an Middle School, had resigned to the Education Department, and the department approved it. The department also appointed a new principal Chen to Huai to take over, scheduled for today (the 16th). However, the students and faculty of the school have a very close relationship with Wang, and they unanimously decided to suspend classes from the 15th. Representatives from both the faculty and students went to the province to petition that the handover could not be temporarily completed. If the petition is effective, of course there will be no problem, otherwise it is heard that all faculty members are prepared to resign en masse, vowing not to cooperate with Chen.

County Magistrate Removed and Loan Recalled: Wang Guodong, the magistrate of Huai'an County, was removed from office by the provincial government and officially handed over today, replaced by the new County Magistrate Wang Zhenyu. However, when Wang was the head of Huai'an, he lent a large sum of money to Huaiyin, 10,000 yuan for the military pay of the forty-ninth division. Now that he has left office, he has no choice but to urge Huaiyin to repay the debt. On the 15th, he sent his staff member Wei to guard and collect the money. The Huaiyin County Government and various agencies found it difficult to raise the huge amount of money in a short time. Yesterday, the county government convened representatives from various agencies to discuss ways to repay the money. As a result, three methods were agreed upon: (1) The representatives of various agencies present on the day jointly telegraphed the provincial government, ordering the Huai'an Customs and the Yangzhou Vehicle Tax Office to allocate the tax money collected to repay the military pay previously borrowed by the forty-ninth division from the local area; (2) The personnel who went to Huai'an to borrow money will still go to Huai'an to declare their responsibility to the various banks for raising the repayment; (3) Continue to collect the money from the households who have recognized but not yet paid the money, and the Huaiyin County Government will issue a receipt to avoid the abuses of floating collection. It is expected that if these steps are followed, the money will be paid off soon.

Jiashan

Detailed Account of the Yangjia Beach Robbery: Regarding the robbery in Yangjia Beach, Xiangfu Dang East, Xitang, yesterday, it is learned that most of the bandits are from Punan, with a total of more than 500 people and more than 30 bandit ships, flying flags embroidered with slogans. This time, a total of six civilian guns and silver and valuables were robbed from Yangjia Beach, and twelve meat tickets, including Xu Sanguan, were taken away. Among those who have not returned are Zhou Longsheng and five or six others. A woman surnamed Xu was forced to offer silver but failed, and a huge stone was added to her body, dying. Xu Yunzhen was also hung and beaten several times until he fainted. A young soybean curd shop girl from a certain surname in Yaozhuang Bridge, about to marry, was taken away by the bandits as the wife of the village. The girl's family is willing to redeem her with silver coins, but the bandits refuse. Yangjia Beach Village was shaken to a total loss of more than 20 civilian boats, with no exact report yet. Zhao Tingyu, the second district chief of the water police, happened to be on a shallow water ship to Xitang for inspection. When he got the news, he led the team to rush there, and the bandits fled to Henggang in the east, causing some disturbances. One branch fled to the Tiantian and Shangxiayun area, hoping to invade Xitang. Last night, there was news that a combined bandit ship from the three villages of the North Gang was heading to Fanbin New Town.

Pinghu

The Prelude to the Automobile Trip from Hangzhou to Zhapu: The Hangzhou-Zhapu Highway is scheduled to open to traffic on April 1. On the 16th, Su, the director of the Works Section of the Provincial Highway Bureau, Li, the director of the Design Section, and Shen Kuiliang, the engineer of the Hangping Section, and other eight people drove two sedan cars and arrived in Zhapu at 3:00 PM to inspect the bridges, and returned to the provincial capital at 5:00 PM, which took only three hours. The test drive ceremony is now scheduled for the 23rd.

Shanghai Class Ships Temporarily Suspended: Yesterday, all kinds of rumors suddenly broke out in the city, saying that the gang of bandits who robbed Xincang had the news of a large-scale robbery. The county government then announced special martial law. In order to avoid danger, all ships to Shanghai temporarily suspended sailing today. It is heard that one ship has already sailed and returned. Because Jinshan is adjacent to the countryside in Pinghu, it seems that bandits have been found. There was a small contact in Maokou last night, and the city is on high alert. Most of the military police were transferred to guard the east gate.

Xiaoshan

Director of the Finance Bureau and Staff Taken to Province: Regarding the arrest of Shen Changyi, Director of the Finance Bureau of Xiaoshan County, and staff members Miao Baoshan and Yu Huixian, the county government received a telegram from the province on the 15th, ordering Shen Changyi, Miao Baoshan, and Yu Huixian to be taken to the province immediately for verification and seizure. After receiving the telegram, the county government sent several police officers in the afternoon to take the three people to the province.

Former County Magistrate Zhao Pays Up the Outstanding Case Money: Zhao Qiang, the former magistrate of Xiaoshan County, still owed 5,020.98 yuan in the handover case and stated that there was still 2,632.674 yuan of silver to be submitted for the case. Yesterday, the Provincial Department of Finance ordered the former County Magistrate Zhao to pay 3,600 yuan.

Night Sailing Overturns and Two Drown: In Xixiao River in Xiaoshan, on the night of the 16th, a night boat from Shaocheng to Linpu overturned due to the rapid current and the rope breaking. All the goods were completely lost, and two boatmen drowned. The next morning, another boat salvaged the bodies, but there was no news yet.

Shangyu

Continued News of the Kidnapping Cases in Tangpu: Wu Yunting in Tangpu Street and Chen Guanshu's six-year-old son in Zhengyan Village, both in Shao, were kidnapped by five or six armed bandits at the same time a few days ago. It is now learned that residents of villages such as Xiaowu and Miaowan, in view of the previous incidents of Chen Guanshu's family, are planning to defend themselves and send strong men to guard strictly until late at night. At first, Wu Yunting was kidnapped on the way home from watching the opera in the town, but his family did not know. Later, when he did not return for several days, he suspected that he had quarreled at home because of trivial matters and ran away to Qi's house to avoid it. It was not until he received a letter from the bandits urging him to go to a certain place in Hangzhou to negotiate the ransom that he knew he had been kidnapped. It was also learned that Chen Guanshu received a letter from the bandits the day before yesterday, demanding 60,000 yuan.

Automobile Highway Expansion Route: Shao Cao Sheng Automobile Company recently plans to extend the route from Haoba to Shangpu. A board meeting was held a few days ago and it was decided to start surveying and measuring next month. After the surveying and measuring is completed, the bidding will start. The route is more than ten miles long and passes through Changshan, Zhangting, Hutou Temple, Meiwu, Qiutanling, Kunlun, and Dashan villages, and reaches Shangpu, where a station will be set up.

Ningbo

Young Woman Dies for Her Fiancé: Lu's eldest daughter, A Ming, 22 years old, at No. 4, Daifu, Lujia Fentou, Jiangbei Bank of Ningbo, is intelligent and has studied since childhood. She dropped out of school two years ago and learned needlework at home, working very diligently and loved by her parents. In January of this year, she was betrothed to Fu Jiemao of Wojia Lane, Jiangbei Bank, to be his second wife. The engagement was completed on the 18th of last month, and the wedding was scheduled for July of this year. Zhang was a staff member of the Bank of China in Hankou, but resigned last year and entered a certain gold shop in Shanghai. He returned to Ningbo three months ago to recuperate due to ill health. Unexpectedly, after arriving home, he passed away suddenly the day before yesterday (the 16th). A Ming cried all night after hearing the bad news, and was so sad that she wanted to die. After her parents, brothers and sisters tried to comfort her in every way, she pretended to restrain her grief. Unexpectedly, yesterday (the 17th) at about 5:00 AM, she went out on the pretext of something and ran to Yongxing Liangmao Hang Lane, jumped into the river, and died. Her body floated to the Jiangmian of Fushiting, where it was spotted by someone and rescued by boat. She was already gasping for breath. Her parents, brothers and sisters rushed to the scene after hearing the news and took her to Huamei Hospital for treatment, but it was too late and she had died. A Ming's parents, because their daughter had died for her husband, planned to carry the coffin to the Qian house and bury it with her fiancé Zhang Jiemao to fulfill the wishes of the deceased.

International Women's Basketball

Federal Wins Against England... 34 to 23

United States Wins Against China... 34 to 12

The Shanghai International Women's Basketball Championship held two games yesterday starting at 6 PM in the Chinese Basketball Hall. As a result, the Federal team won against England 34 to 23, and the United States won against China 34 to 12.

(1) Federal Wins Against the United States

Both Teams Performed Well

Starting at six o'clock, Miss. Jie Hansheng of the Federal team was brave and skilled, a rare talent. At the start of the game, Miss Jie scored four consecutive goals, and the Federal team took an 8-0 lead. Afterwards, although England tried its best to attack, it was difficult to catch up. The first quarter was 9 to 5, the second quarter was even with 8 points each, the third quarter was 5 to 2, and the fourth quarter was 12 to 8, all in favor of the Federal team. The overall result was that the Federal team won 34 to 23. The referee was Mr. Smith. The performance of both teams was very agile and excellent.

(2) United States Wins Against China

The Chinese Team's Formation Was Disorganized

Yesterday, the Chinese team's formation was disorganized, with no sense of cooperation. Moreover, each player was short and weak. Facing the tall and large American team was truly like striking a stone with an egg. The skill gap was vast. Shi Fuyi and Chen Xinyuan were the central defensive pillars, but their performance last night was also less agile than expected. The forwards, who usually pride themselves on their courage, became flustered when faced with such a strong opponent. Grabbing, dodging, and avoiding shots lacked their usual ease and experience. In addition, the entire team frequently committed fouls, giving the opponent counterattack opportunities. Compared to the initial games, their skills not only did not improve but seemed to have regressed. The American team's talent was evenly distributed, and their teamwork was far superior to China's. They were often able to seize opportunities and attack China's weaknesses, leading to a clear victory. In the initial exchanges, the United States took a high lead of 10 to 3 in the first quarter. They continued to lead in the second quarter with 10 to 2. In the third quarter, Chen Xinyuan was reassigned to center, scoring two goals in succession. However, Crier scored three consecutive goals for the opposing team. The fourth quarter was particularly intense. Three points were briefly scored, and Ms. Chen and Ms. Guo advanced together. In a short time, the opposing team scored another seven points, resulting in a final score of 34 to 12. The international team won. In the battle between England and the Federal team, both sides were evenly matched. However, in the last quarter, the agile English women reversed the situation and won with a score of 34 to 23.

Jingzhi Wins the Women's Volleyball Championship

Yesterday, Two Sets to Zero Against Jingzhong

Attending the National Games

Jingzhi Wins First Set: The women's volleyball Jingzhi team won the championship. The participants in the women's volleyball competition included Suzhou Zhongxue, Jingzhong, Jingzhi, and Zhenhua. Since the beginning of the competition, Jingzhi initially won two sets to zero against Suzhou Zhongxue. At the same time, Jingzhong also won two sets to zero against Zhenhua. At 2:00 PM on the 19th, Jingzhi and Jingzhong competed for the championship. The referee was Xu Shaowu. The skills of the two teams have long been renowned, and countless spectators watched. Both sides were full of energy and excellent skills. As the whistle sounded, Jingzhi immediately gained the upper hand with powerful serves. Furthermore, the team's coordination was excellent, and the score quickly soared. Initially, Jingzhong tried hard to resist, scoring three points in the first half. Jingzhi took the lead with a score of 11 to 3. In the second half, with a change of sides, Jingzhi continued to attack with high-pressure serves, horizontal strikes, and diagonal shots, sweeping all before them. Soon, they won the first set 21 to 3.

Jingzhi Wins Second Set: Jingzhi's spirit remained strong, and their momentum increased. They took an 11 to 1 lead in the first half. In the second half, Jingzhong showed great brilliance, rushing to catch up with all their might. The situation improved, and they gradually entered a better state. However, they suddenly stopped progressing after scoring eleven points. Jingzhi's spirit doubled, and they became invincible, winning the second set against Suzhou Zhongxue with a score of 21 to 11. They were awarded the title of champion for women and will represent the school at the National Games.

Jingzhi Team Roster: Instructor Sun Chaoxiong; First Row: Gu Peiming, Wu Ruoxi, Ding Yunshang, Yang Subao; Second Row: Rong Meiyun, Hou Yufen, Tong Wende (Captain), Huang Qiangying; Third Row: Qin Duanbao, Lu Yingxi, Yao Ruolan, Zhang Jinrong; Reserves: Xue Xing, Ding Zhijuan, Chen Yuying

China Prepares to Participate in the Far Eastern Games

Raising Departure Funds of 80,000, Excellent Results

Overseas Chinese in Japan and Lin Zhuguang Are Willing to Host

Reviewing New Sports Rules for Training

Training After the National Games Concludes

The upcoming Far Eastern Games, scheduled to be held in Tokyo, Japan, on May 24th, have prompted active preparations in various provinces and cities across China. Outstanding talents are being selected and strong teams are being formed, ready to compete against the heroes of the three islands and the skilled athletes of the Philippines. Consequently, the buzz surrounding sports events has been shaking the nation, filled with vigor and excitement, marking an unprecedented prosperous scene in the Republic of China's history. It is indeed a good omen for the future of sports in our country. The progress of preparations to participate in the Far Eastern Games has been reported in several newspapers. Now, the most recent updates are explored below:

Economic Aspects

The most crucial issue for participating in the Far Eastern Games is finance. The China National Amateur Athletic Federation, responsible for this task, focused on this matter from the beginning. A detailed budget was prepared, totaling at least 80,000 or more. Although Chairman Jiang of the National Government generously donated 40,000 yuan (20,000 yuan has been allocated to Hao Boyang, a key member of the Federation), a significant shortfall remains. Therefore, the Federation has sent letters and telegrams to prominent figures in the country and enthusiastic sports supporters among overseas Chinese, inviting them to assist with fundraising. Economic directors from various sectors both domestically and abroad were appointed to solicit donations, hoping to gather enough to support this grand undertaking. It is reported that favorable responses have been received from various locations, with quite good results.

Hospitality

There are numerous Chinese compatriots traveling to Japan for business. At each Far Eastern Games held in Japan, they generously contribute funds to organize large-scale reception venues to welcome fellow athletes, showing their patriotic enthusiasm that truly inspires endless admiration. The upcoming games will again be held in Tokyo. The Federation has sent letters requesting Ambassador Wang Rongbao in Japan, as well as the Chinese Associations in Tokyo, Kobe, Osaka, and other locations, to handle hospitality matters. It is reported that wealthy merchants among overseas Chinese have readily assumed responsibility, forming reception committees to prepare for a grand welcome at the time.

It is also reported that Mr. Lin Zhuguang, a wealthy businessman from Luzon, Philippines, is one of the key economic directors of the Federation. He is currently overseas, soliciting substantial donations to provide financial support. During the 7th Far Eastern Games held in the Philippines, Mr. Lin spent tens of thousands on hosting the Chinese athletes, bringing glory to the country. This time, he will also do his best to assist the Federation and support this grand event, planning to return to China on the 4th to accompany the athletes to Japan.

Rules

The rules of various sports in the Far Eastern Games inevitably change with trends. Therefore, the Federation has hired top domestic sports experts to review the suitability of various sports rules and establish standards for future athlete training, in preparation for on-site competitions.

Training Aspects

The day the Hangzhou National Games conclude will be the time when the representatives for our China Far Eastern Games are selected. There will still be more than a month until the opening of the Games, allowing ample time for the athletes to practice thoroughly. Therefore, the issues of guidance and management for the athletes before their departure are extremely important. It is heard that the Association authorities are currently in the process of finding suitable housing for the athletes to stay in. At that time, they will hire specialized personnel with profound knowledge and rich experience to take on the responsibility of providing guidance. Regarding management matters, they advocate for strict enforcement in order to conserve energy and build strength, and to enhance national glory.

News on the Preparations for the National Education Conference

Liu Dabai, Chairman of the Preparatory Committee for the National Education Conference, believing that the conference was imminent, convened a meeting of all the Preparatory Committee officials at the Ministry of Education's conference room at 2:00 PM on the 18th. More than 20 people attended, including the Chairman, Vice-Chairman, Standing Committee members, department heads, and staff. Chaired by Liu Dabai, it was decided that the office would begin operations at the Club from that day onwards. Subsequently, at 3:00 PM each afternoon, one staff member from each department (document administration, reception, editing, accounting, etc.) would be assigned daily on a rotating basis to work at the preparatory office, to take on designated responsibilities.

Free Talk

One Man's Opinion

— Wei

If there were no cosmetics in the world, at least one-third of the young men and women worldwide would be saved.

If the emotional energy spent between men and women were instead focused on saving the nation and the party, then revolutionary success could be achieved imminently.

If women absolutely could not reproduce, then women's rights in the world would be higher than anything else.

Men look down on women, while women look up to men.

A man views his newlywed wife like a newly tailored Western suit.

The heart awaiting a lover's rendezvous is like the heart of a sentry on the front lines.

A virgin's heart is a spiderweb. A man is a dragonfly.

If the footprints a lover leaves on the ground could be collected, then someone would surely lie on the ground and pick them up step by step. Listening to a lover's voice is more attentive than hearing the sound of an ant crawling on the ground.

A man thinks he has made her his plaything, just as a woman thinks she has made him her plaything. In the same way, they unknowingly play with each other, and each believes themselves to be the victor.

In Memory of Physical Educationist Wei Xudong

— Zheng Yimei

Mr. Wei Xudong was a native of Hunan. He initially served in the military, earning a reputation for his bravery and skill in battle. Later, he retired from the army and enjoyed traveling through mountains and rivers in straw sandals. He admired the wonders of Tiger Hill and Lingyan Temple in Suzhou, lingering for a long time, seemingly forgetting his home. Dongwu University, the highest institution of learning in Suzhou, and Caoqiao Middle School then hired him to teach military science and physical education. Mr. Wei, having come from a military background, was not highly literate. When teaching military science, he often mispronounced words in the lecture notes. However, his reasoning was exceptionally clear, his experience exceptionally rich, and his witty remarks were constant. His mistakes were overlooked. Mr. Wei was skilled in the use of the iron bar. He could lift a large cauldron on the bar, again and again, eventually swinging his body around it. The iron bar, as thick as a child's arm, would bend, yet Mr. Wei would not even pant or sweat. When teaching military drills, he often led the team to the suburbs. When it rained heavily, some students would hesitate and try to avoid it. Mr. Wei would immediately scold them, saying, "If a man does not first forge and temper his body, how will he become a pillar of the nation in the future?" The students, hearing this, would feel emboldened, braced themselves, and battled the rain. Their bodies would be drenched, but they became accustomed to it. The people of Suzhou were generally weak, and the customs changed as a result. Mr. Wei was also skilled in shooting. During his free time on Sundays, he often went out with a hunting gun. Even if the birds flew high, Mr. Wei never missed. In the slanting rays of the setting sun, one could see spotted doves and pheasants hanging on the end of his gun. Then, Mr. Wei would return home. Mr. Wei also enjoyed riding donkeys. When riding swiftly, he would leap off the saddle in a single bound, leaving the donkey to wander freely. Then, he would chase after it and, just as the donkey was running, Mr. Wei would already be sitting on top of it again. However, the donkey's strength was limited and it often became exhausted as a result. The donkey driver would not allow it, so Mr. Wei would double his payment. One day, Mr. Wei went to Tiger Hill with his students. He saw a beggar catching snakes. Mr. Wei gave him money to release the snake. The snake quickly disappeared into the grass. Mr. Wei then paid the beggar to chase after it again. After it was caught, he released it again. Releasing it and chasing it again, Mr. Wei found it amusing. He enjoyed playing around in this way. One day, a former student asked a famous calligrapher who taught Chinese to write a couplet. Mr. Wei saw it, snatched it away, and offered himself instead. The students thought that the couplet was doomed, that it would just be scribbled on and used as scrap paper. Unexpectedly, Mr. Wei dipped his brush in ink and completed it in a moment. The strokes were bold and upright, resembling the Northern Wei style. The students were greatly surprised and impressed. It turned out that Mr. Wei had been secretly studying calligraphy from stone tablets for a long time, but he had kept it a secret and had not revealed it before. From then on, he received more and more requests for his calligraphy. Mr. Wei was unable to respond to them all, so he set a fee to limit the requests. Mr. Wei also served as the commander of the merchant militia for several years. Therefore, even women and children knew his great name. Since I took up residence in Shanghai, I have not heard about Mr. Wei's condition for a long time. Yesterday, my schoolmate Wang Ziqing came to visit and said that Mr. Wei had become very depressed due to some event. He indulged in alcohol and women to distract himself, fell ill, and returned to Hunan. He has now passed away. It is a pity.

A Visit to Liu and Zhang's Wedding

— Wang Meiju

On March 16th, Ms. Zhang Shiyi, the daughter of the respected elder Mr. Zhang Yishan, and Mr. Liu Hairuo, the younger brother of the famous painter Liu Haisu and a teacher at the Shanghai Fine Arts School, held their wedding ceremony at the Central Hotel on Wuma Road. Meiju has always admired Mr. Zhang Yishan as a teacher, and Ms. Zhang Shiqiu's younger sister, Shizhao, once sought calligraphy lessons from me. Therefore, I was able to attend and observe the grand ceremony. In my opinion, purely old-style weddings are no longer seen today. Civilized or semi-civilized styles are seen intermittently. Today's Liu-Zhang wedding cannot be separated from civilization, and the harmony in the hall, with both new and old elements, made the couple even more beautiful. Therefore, I am happy to record it.

The Truth of Perfect Beauty Ms. Zhang Shiqiu is a talented student at the Shanghai Fine Arts School. It is said that Mr. Hairuo and Ms. Shiqiu were classmates who became teachers and students, and then went from teachers and students to becoming husband and wife. This is the source of perfect beauty. Hairuo's appearance is majestic and spirited, with none of the frivolousness of worldly young men. Shiqiu, on the other hand, is dignified and graceful. They walked side by side during the ceremony, calm and composed, and their strength and gracefulness complemented each other. Can this not be called the truth of perfect beauty?

The Lady's Knowledge of Propriety Mrs. Zhang has many children. She has assisted Mr. Yishan in managing the household affairs and educating the children for a long time, and has a long-standing reputation. On this day, Mr. Yishan had just recovered from a minor illness and was unable to personally preside over the ceremony. Mrs. Zhang expressed her apologies and gratitude to the guests in a humble and respectful manner, which moved those who heard it. My female disciple, Zhang Shizhao, walked back and forth, carefully considering everything. Her filial piety was evident in her eyebrows. With parents like these, it is fitting that they have such a daughter.

The Variety of Guests On this day, the male and female guests were diverse and colorful. Mr. Yishan is a respected elder, so there were scholars with both age and virtue. Ms. Zhang Shiqiu is a talented student at the Shanghai Fine Arts School, so there were young people with unique attire. Among the virtuous men, Mr. Yu Zhaokang was the oldest, arriving with a cane, his beard and eyebrows faintly exuding a Taoist aura. Mr. Qu Wenliu is also a famous figure of the Republic of China, attending because of local friendship. Many of the female guests were from old-fashioned families, and their conversations were elegant. It is a pity that Meiju is neither new nor old, and felt a bit out of place among them.

The Amusing Words at the Feast The guests entered the banquet at six o'clock. The female guests were seated in the east corner, and the male guests were seated in the west. One guest joked, "The women's circle is not just seeking equality with the men's circle." The words were quite amusing. A moment later, the newlywed couple gracefully arrived and offered wine to each table. Everyone accepted and drank, daring not to refuse. The second table on the west seemed to be occupied by Hairuo's classmates. Hairuo then went to another person and socialized with this table. One guest at the table forced Hairuo to play the finger-guessing game. Hairuo declined, asking the guest to represent him. The guest said, "Can finger-guessing be represented? Can everything you are doing today also be represented by me?" Everyone laughed, and Hairuo dared not refuse again. What amusing words!

Seeing Little and Wondering Much A congratulatory banner had the four characters "Yi Qi Zhou Jia" (宜其州家). I asked people but they all said they did not know. I asked Shizhao, and Shizhao said, "The gold characters are in a box, and that's what's written on the box." As I was about to enter the banquet, Meiju was still troubled by these four characters, like a bone stuck in my throat. I hurried to ask Mr. Wang and his well-spoken wife, hoping to gain some insight, but the two were busy hosting the female guests, so I did not ask. There is no shortage of erudite people in the world, and they must laugh at my seeing little and wondering much.

New Talk on Swindling

— Zheng

Shanghai is a place where people from all directions gather, so there are especially many bizarre things. Recently, my friend encountered a swindling case, which was also quite interesting. I'm writing it out for you all to see, so you can avoid being deceived.

One night, my friend Mr. C was sitting in his study. Suddenly, a middle-aged man came in, dressed neatly and not resembling a low-class person. He was also very respectful. Although Mr. C was surprised because he didn't know him, he had to exchange a few pleasantries with him. Listening to his accent, it was clearly from the same hometown. He also admitted that he lived not far from Mr. C's house. He said that he had been away for many years and had always been living in the army. He was currently a battalion commander under a certain military commander and would be leaving soon. He used to be very familiar with Mr. C's father in the South, and he even described Mr. C's father's situation at the time, the family situation, and even his personality in detail. Mr. C thought that he was an old friend of his father, so of course he didn't dare to neglect him and treated him sincerely. Who knew that after talking for a while, he suddenly took out two pawn tickets, one for seven yuan and one for thirteen yuan. He said that because he had been staying in Shanghai for a long time, life was very difficult. As soon as the weather cleared up, he had to put his robe in the pawn shop. How could he meet people in short clothes (he was wearing a raincoat when he came)? So now he was willing to pledge one seven-yuan pawn ticket to you for nine yuan, so that he could redeem his robe. This seven-yuan pawn ticket was for a brand new Western suit, worth at least thirty yuan. You can redeem it. Mr. C thought that he was in dire straits and was also a friend of his father in the past, so of course he lent him the money. So he gave him nine yuan and immediately wrote a letter to tell his father. Who knew that three days later, his father replied, saying that this person was a rascal, specializing in swindling. He had previously swindled him out of two yuan. Only then did Mr. C realize that he had been scammed. But it was too late to regret. Later, Mr. C met many relatives and friends, who all said that they had been scammed by this person, and that he had borrowed in Mr. C's name. As for that pawn ticket, Mr. C was afraid of causing more trouble, so he didn't want to redeem it.

After hearing this, I couldn't help but have some thoughts. Just imagine these swindlers, who have a good appearance and good eloquence. Why do they fall to such a state? Who is to blame? What led to this? It really makes me feel infinitely emotional.

Warmth in the Heart (152)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 9: The Celebrities Make a Racket Playing Hide-and-Seek, A Beautiful Woman Willfully Provides Support

It can be seen that the playful games also followed the national system. In that Chinese national system, before the reforms to democracy, the flower world also used the imperial system. Therefore, there were titles like Pheasant King and Me King. Later, after the group republic, those gentlemen who joked and wrote started what they called the Flower World Election. At that time, there was no longer the feminine air of the Great King, so they elected what they called the Flower World President. For a time, Shanghai had several Flower World Presidents, all of whom were in the limelight. Even the brothels in Hangzhou and Suzhou followed suit. This is a later story. Now, let me say that in addition to the Me King, there was also a tall and elegant woman, with the air of a tall and beautiful woman. Do you know who she is? Her name was Hongbing Xiaoxie. This was highly appreciated by Shi Guanping. Originally, most women were short and small, especially the so-called beauties. Those who praised them called them petite and exquisite. Indeed, large women did not qualify as beauties. But the appearance of a short, fat person was also disgusting. Tall and elegant was indeed desirable. As long as she was not too thin. Thin and tall was like a bamboo pole. It had to be well-proportioned. It was like writing characters. It was just that being plump and smooth was better. Hongbing Xiaoxie was one of those who were plump and smooth. In short, she was a beautiful woman with a healthy body. Today, she also came to see the horse races and take pictures. The Mingjing Club was lively enough with this group of people. With the addition of Yan Yichen, Zheng Yanxiu, Shi Guanping, and Zuo Shichen, who often came here, the horse races were naturally more comfortable and pleasant than the stands on the racecourse side of Ma Huo Road. At that time, along Jing'an Temple Road around the racetrack, I don't know where all these people came from. They used long benches and wooden planks to build platforms. Chairs were set up on the platforms. If someone wanted to watch the horse races from their platforms, they had to pay a certain fee. Generally, people from the upper classes who came to watch the horse races hired carriages. The carriages were also decorated with ribbons. Because there were still very few cars at that time. Some also booked large dining rooms, such as Yipinxiang, and brought their wives, daughters, and concubines to enjoy the distant view. Those who sat on the wooden platforms were some villagers from the surrounding areas of Shanghai, such as Pudong, Jiangwan, Minhang, and Yinxiang Port. There were also some small family daughters. Because during the horse racing season, factories were closed and customs were sealed. Those silk factory workers and yarn workers, as well as many shopkeepers, called their aunts and sisters, also had to enjoy themselves in time. Sometimes, there were too many people on the platforms. With a loud crash, the platform collapsed, causing everyone to applaud and cheer. Fortunately, the platform was not built high, so it was not enough to injure people. However, it was common for people to fall down. It was nothing to be surprised about.

Travel Notes from Nanyang (12)

— Linghua

Many families in Guangdong also worship Guan Gong. Now, most of them have changed to hanging portraits of Sun Yat-sen. This is because of the expansion of nationalism.

Generally speaking, the self-governing organizations of our overseas Chinese in Annam are roughly as follows:

(1) Associations: Fujian Association, Guangzhou Zhao Association, Hakka Association, Chaozhou Association, others,

General Chamber of Commerce (2) Occupation: Rice Merchants, Medicine Merchants, Agriculture, Industry, Education, Newspaper Offices,

(3) Social Organizations: 1. Newspaper Offices, 2. Bookstores, 3. Schools, 4. Private Schools, 5. Religions (Buddhism, Christianity), 6. Sports, 7. Fine Arts, 8. Music. The above are just a few things I have heard and seen. However, I sincerely hope that they will connect and help each other, and study in depth the academic knowledge of self-government, in order to seek survival and evolution.

In recent days, various newspapers have reported that Annamese soldiers in the Northern Territory rebelled and injured two French military officers. The French government has also allowed the publication. These are all translated from French newspapers. Now that Japan in the East has risen, and Siam is an independent country, the independence of the Philippines will soon be successful. India, Burma, and Annam all want autonomy. It is not difficult to imagine the future of Nanyang. Last year, when I was in Nanning, Guangxi, there was an old man who had fought in the Sino-French War in the late Qing Dynasty. He still spoke with enthusiasm and stroked his palms about his success in defeating the French. Annam is close to Guangxi and Yunnan. If the country is unified, the communication between overseas Chinese will also be very easy to handle. Alas, I earnestly hope for peace and unification within the country.

The climate in Saigon is usually 80 degrees Fahrenheit. Now is the time to eat watermelons, which are not very large, but are sweet.

Annam is located between 7 degrees and 23 degrees north latitude. It is 3,000 miles long from north to south and 1,200 miles wide from east to west. It is closely connected to Qinlian in Guangdong, Longzhou in Guangxi, and Mengzi in Yunnan. It faces Hainan Island across a stretch of water. The land is fertile and the people are simple and honest. Rice is harvested twice a year. The relationship between China and Annam is close. Guangdong is like Fengtian, while Guangxi and Cochin are like Jilin and Heilongjiang. Its historical relationship dates back to the time of Tang and Yu, when Yuechang had already translated and came to pay tribute to the white pheasant. The Qin Dynasty established the Lin Yi Prefecture and moved people there. The Han Dynasty established the Jiaozhi, Jiuzhen, and Rinan Prefectures. It was not a foreign vassal state, but a prefecture and county.

In the Sino-French Treaty of Guangxu Eleventh Year, China recognized Vietnam as a French protectorate. The political relationship between the two countries was severed.

Common Sense Gleanings

— Tang Bihua

When taking clothes to the laundry for washing, first search the pockets for money and important items. This is a very ordinary thing, but I have been tricked several times.

It is best to go to the same store to inquire about prices. The so-called "compare goods from three stores and you won't suffer a loss" is what this means.

When getting into a rickshaw, first memorize the number on the magnetic plate. In case you lose something in the car, you can report it to the police. It can be found immediately, and there is no case of it not being returned. When getting a haircut at the barbershop, do not ask the barber to clean your ears, do your eyes, or massage your back. Not only is it unhygienic, but it will also cost you more in tips.

New News of this Year's Foreign Dollar

There is normally a period of selling for late March and mid-April in which the deals and amounts are very large. But since the stop deals of last year, sometimes secret deals were made. But this year, there is no secret deal. According to news from industry, a raw silk foreign firm wished to pre-purchase late-April (around the end of March and the beginning of April) of the Gregorian calendar from a Qian firm. There were several millions of potential purchases and they wanted to pay a high price of 7 qian, 2 fen, and 2 li and a half. As a result, the supplier didn't want to, and no deal was made. It's heard that the Qian firm side guessed that that the price would go above that at the time and so it didn't want to. If the purchasing party was willing to pay 7 qian, 2 fen and 5 li, then possibly 1-2 million could be traded. However, even this cannot be fully supplied. From this it can be known how hard it is to do secret deals this year and it is determined that there are no major deals.

Grain: White Rice Reaches 20 Yuan

Zhabei: Yesterday, only a dozen ships arrived from various routes. The market was extremely active. Common white rice from Changbang rose sharply by about two jiao. Medium-grade northern rice also increased by 1.5 to 2.5 jiao. The market price for specially high-grade rice was 19 yuan and 9.5 jiao, reaching the 20 yuan mark. This price can be called a groundbreaking new record. If the weather turns overcast, prices may continue to rise. Thin rice arrivals were scarce and sales were flat. Yangdu indica rice, due to frequent increases in foreign prices, attracted attention from shopkeepers, and prices rose by one to two jiao. Various indica rice from other ports were particularly attractive because customers from inland routes were actively purchasing, and arrivals at Shanghai port were scarce. Retail sales were competitive, and merchants were bartering and selling, keeping the market tight. Changing to cash made the local market feel refreshed, and the trend was lively, with prices rising nearly a jiao.

South Shanghai: Arrivals from the river area were not strong, and the sales market continued to be active. Common japonica rice from Suzhou, Tongcheng, and other areas was experiencing fewer sources due to special customers in inland production areas purchasing and hoarding, leading to daily increases in quoted prices. Shanghai merchants, who had to transport the rice from further away, faced increased costs and firmly held onto higher prices, pushing the market higher and higher. Yesterday, prices rose sharply by another 1.5 jiao. Ordinary high-grade rice in this area was also above the 19 yuan mark. Thin early rice such as Qingjiao from southern areas gradually gained attention from shops, as rice prices were still at a relatively low level, making purchases attractive. Prices rose by about a jiao. Arrivals of Yangdu indica rice were light, and rural sales were very strong, leading to demand exceeding supply. In addition, frequent increases in Saigon small rice also contributed to the rise of local indica rice by 1.5 jiao. White rice showed slight continued strength, but sales were not active.

Flour Price: Recently 5 Qian Entering Customs

A Certain Factory Sells 40-50 Thousand Bags

Yesterday, when the flour market opened in the morning, the quoted price of foreign wheat was slightly better, and people's sentiment was quite stable. However, there were signs of unrest in the situation, and merchants inevitably became cautious. At that time, a certain factory was selling well for March and April, estimated to be between 40-50 thousand bags. As a result, people's sentiment was very weak in the near-term months, and April was entering customs at 5 qian. When the market opened in the afternoon, the price for this month once fell to 2 taels and 5 qian. Later, Tianjin merchants slightly increased their purchases, and Hankou also slightly covered their short positions, so the market recovered and stabilized. The prices for other months were generally hovering. Considering the future steps, if the north is not stable, the future of the flour market may be impacted. As a result, the prices for March, April, and May were each 7.5 li lower than the previous day, the price for June was unchanged, and the prices for July and August were each 2.5 li lower.

Futures Wheat: Mixed Increases and Decreases

Yesterday, after the opening of the futures wheat market in the morning and afternoon, there were mixed increases and decreases in the prices for various months. The price for this month was high because the delivery date was approaching, and although short sellers had physical goods, only half of them met the standards of the exchange. Therefore, sellers who did not meet the standards had to cover their positions, which is why the market price increased. The sentiment for new wheat in various months was very good, and buying was strong, leading to a sudden surge in the market. As a result, the price for this month was 4 fen higher than the previous month, the price for April was 1 fen lower, the price for June was 2 fen higher, the price for July was 1 fen higher, and the price for August was 2 fen higher. In the spot market, high-quality goods were rarely seen for delivery, and medium and low-quality wheat dominated. Wheat from Kainan and Suxiu was 5 taels and 7 fen, and wheat from Jiangxi was 4 taels, 6 qian, 3 fen to 4 qian, with a total of 1,200 bags purchased by Fufeng.

Futures Foreign Rice Soars Unceasingly

Yesterday, futures foreign rice was even more remarkably popular, rising more than 1 qian compared to the previous day. Rice from the Lu route rose by nearly 2 jiao, and spot prices also rose by 1 jiao. The reason for the increase was that foreign firms were still selling, and there were rumors of an incident in the Raikong area, making it impossible to pre-sell in the future. Another part of the foreign firms settled prices with Shanghai merchants, and people unanimously expected the market to improve, leading to a surge in futures prices. The market sold 3,000 bags of number 1 Saigon rice, 2,000 bags of number 3 rice, and 1,000 bags of Qiafo rice in total, and more than 30,000 bags of futures were sold, all of which were covering positions.

(1) Since our party launched the Northern Expedition from Guangdong in July of the 15th year of the Republic of China, the military strength has been sharp and swift, like a bamboo shoot, and successively occupied Hunan, Hubei, Fujian, Jiangxi, and directly pointed to Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Shandong. He temporarily settled in Wuhan and personally led armed comrades to seize Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Shanghai is the most important city in the country, and its economic, situational, and public opinion influence is sufficient to affect the overall situation. Therefore, it is a battleground for revolutionary and counter-revolutionary forces. At that time, the Shanghai Communists, under the orders of their cadres, vigorously opposed the advance into Jiangsu and Zhejiang and squeezed out responsible comrades of our party in Shanghai everywhere. Furthermore, they secretly plotted to sabotage. Fortunately, the spirit of the Premier in heaven and the unity of the people allowed us to avoid being swayed by conspiracies. On March 20 of the 16th year of the Republic of China (i.e., 1927), the National Revolutionary Army arrived at Longhua, and the rebel army began to retreat. Our army completely occupied Shanghai. All secret work came to an end. We should know that when our party launched the Northern Expedition, the Communist Party initially opposed it. When opposition failed, they obstructed it. When obstruction failed, they ultimately destroyed it. Their conspiracy was aimed at overthrowing our party and only then would they be satisfied. Therefore, today, for the sake of consolidating our party and realizing the Three People's Principles, we must eliminate the Communist Party members and all quasi-communist remnants, such as the reorganization faction, so that we will not betray the past sacrifices of the Northern Expedition soldiers of our party, and the Three People's Principles will have a day to be realized.

(2) The recovery of Shanghai relied half on military victory and half on the struggle of the revolutionary masses. Looking back, the rebel army relied on the ports of Shanghai and stubbornly resisted. Therefore, the struggle of our revolutionary masses has made great contributions. Since establishing the capital in Nanjing, we have strived forward with this purpose and completed the Northern Expedition in a year.
