However, Gui, Feng, Zhang, and Tang successively rebelled. Fortunately, the spirit of the Premier and the efforts of our comrades succeeded in eliminating them. If the skin does not exist, what will the fur adhere to? For the sake of safeguarding today's glory, we must only develop the spirit of eliminating the rebel army in those years and continue our efforts.

March 22 is only the work of destructively eliminating the remaining rebel army, and its purpose is to build a new Shanghai based on the party's doctrine, policies, and political programs. British Postal Service Sticks Stamps on Each Letter

Crackdown on Private Postal Agencies' Consolidated Packages

To be Implemented on April 1

Regarding the British-controlled Kuala Lumpur Postal Service's crackdown on private postal agencies' consolidated package method, it was previously reported that overseas Chinese representatives stated that this was initiated by the Chinese postal service. The Chinese postal service sent a telegram to inquire, and its reply was recorded in the previous report. It is now learned that the British-controlled Kuala Lumpur Postal Service has sent a letter to the Chinese postal service stating that after March 31st, all consolidated package letters from private postal agencies must be fully charged at the rate of the Universal Postal Union for each item. All overseas Chinese have been notified. The letter from the British-controlled Kuala Lumpur Postal Service and its notice are recorded as follows:

Letter: The British-controlled Kuala Lumpur Postal Service letter dated March 5 (No. 1984.1929) states: "We received your postal service's telegram dated March 1st, stating: 'Regarding the consolidated package method of private postal agencies, our government has received a petition from the All-Overseas Chinese Congress, strongly opposing it, and claiming that the Governor of Singapore, the Superintendent of Chinese Affairs, and the postal authorities issued letters proving that this proposal was initiated by our government. Please reply with details of the situation at the time.'" After receiving the telegram, a reply was sent on the same day as follows: "We have received your telegram. Regarding the private postal agency case, when the Chinese representatives were received at the Singapore Governor's Office on January 20th, our office did not say that the proposal to abolish the special preferential treatment of consolidated packages from private postal agencies was initiated by the Chinese government." When the Chinese representatives were received, the Governor clearly notified the representatives that the government's decision on the case of cracking down on the consolidated package system of private postal agencies was to be implemented as soon as possible after the preparations were completed. The representatives reversed the facts and claimed that the Governor told them that this crackdown was initiated by your government, which is regrettable. The representatives reversed the facts in order to retain the preferential treatment of private postal agencies, which is deeply regrettable. It is now decided that after March 31st of this year, all postage must be fully charged at the rate of the Universal Postal Union for each item. The governments of the Nanyang Islands and the Malay Peninsula have issued two notices to inform the public. Two copies of the notices are enclosed for your reference."

Notice: (1) Government Gazette No. 10 of the Nanyang Islands Government, February 7, 1930, Postal Notice No. 236 of the Nanyang Islands Postal Service, for notice: Consolidated package letters from private postal agencies sent from the post offices of the Nanyang Islands to China for delivery shall be affixed with stamps for each item after March 31st of this year. The charge for the first ounce is 12 cents, and an additional 6 cents for each additional ounce or fraction thereof. Notice No. 844 published in the Gazette of April 30, 1924, shall be cancelled immediately. Please take note. (2) Government Gazette No. 1256 of the Federated Malay States Government, February 14, 1930, Postal Notice No. 25 of the Federated Malay States Postal Service, for notice: Consolidated package letters from private postal agencies sent from the Federated Malay States to China for delivery shall be affixed with stamps for each item after March 31st of this year. The charge for the first ounce is 12 cents, and an additional 6 cents for each additional ounce or fraction thereof. Please take note.

Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Urges Shanghai Gas Company to Sign a Contract

The British-owned Shanghai Gas Company has enjoyed the right to operate in the Chinese territory for many years but has not fulfilled its responsibilities. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities, as the competent authority, has repeatedly negotiated with the company to sign a contract to determine its rights and obligations. Unexpectedly, the company has remained evasive, and the case has been suspended for more than a year. On January 29th of this year, the two sides once again continued negotiations and largely agreed on the contract terms. The bureau then drafted a Chinese contract based on the results of the talks and instructed the company to decide before February 15th. It then repeatedly urged the company by letter, but the company never gave a concrete reply. The bureau, considering its deliberate delay, had to resort to a decisive course of action. However, for the sake of prudence, it reported to the municipal government for consideration and sent a letter to the company yesterday solemnly declaring that three weeks from the date of the letter would be the final consideration period. Municipal Government Promulgates the Regulations of the Municipal Agricultural Experiment Field

After the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs selected Fahua Temple in Luhang District as the site for the Municipal Agricultural Experiment Field, it has been actively proceeding. Recently, in order to have rules to follow in its affairs, the bureau specially drafted nine articles of regulations, which have been presented to the municipal government for amendment and promulgation. The regulations are recorded below: Article 1: This field is subordinate to the Shanghai Special City Bureau of Social Affairs. Article 2: This field shall temporarily limit itself to the cultivation and experimentation of major agricultural crops such as cotton, rice, and wheat, and shall be responsible for the following matters: 1. Regarding the cultivation and experimentation of cotton, rice, and wheat, and breeding; 2. Regarding the fertilizer experimentation of cotton, rice, and wheat; 3. Regarding the prevention and control of diseases and insect pests of cotton, rice, and wheat; 4. Regarding the guidance and consultation of agricultural crops in the urban area; 5. Regarding the distribution of agricultural crop seeds in the urban area; 6. Regarding agricultural surveys and research; 7. Regarding climate reports; 8. Regarding other agricultural experiments and research. Article 3: The staff of this field shall be as follows: 1. One director; 2. Several technicians and assistant technicians; 3. Several clerks. Article 4: The director, with the permission of the director of the Bureau, shall be responsible for all affairs of the field and shall direct and supervise the staff under his supervision. Technicians and assistant technicians, with the permission of the director of the Bureau and the director of the field, shall handle technical matters. Clerks, with the permission of the director of the field, shall handle documents, accounting, and general affairs. Article 5: The director and technicians shall be appointed by the mayor upon the recommendation of the director of the Bureau of Social Affairs. Article 6: Assistant technicians and clerks shall be appointed by the director of the Bureau. Article 7: When necessary, this field may establish branch fields. Article 8: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, they may be presented for amendment at any time. Article 9: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation by the Special Municipal Government.

To Be Implemented on April 1

The Shanghai County Government issued a notice yesterday, stating that it had previously received instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, stating that it had received instructions from the Provincial Government, stating that the Department had submitted a memorial to the Provincial Government on whether the Land Guard system should be abolished, including a clear memorial on the opinions of each county, and that the original duties of the Land Guards should be managed by the Township Public Offices, and that this malpractice should be abolished quickly and resolutely by ordering its abolition, so as to avoid disturbing the people and hindering the instruction and training of government affairs. It should be noted that, in accordance with the instructions, it should be reported to the Department of Civil Affairs for review and approval, and the County Finance Bureau and the district chiefs should be ordered to comply with the notice to the people of the county. Zhao Tieqiao's Suggestions Regarding the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company

The Best Plan: Nationalize it.

The Middle Plan: National Management.

The Worst Plan: Joint Public-Private Management.

Zhao Tieqiao suggested to the Third Plenary Session: "In order to fundamentally resolve the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company issue, I earnestly request your consideration and adoption of the following suggestions for implementation. This will promote the spirit of the Party, revitalize national shipping, facilitate significant construction, and enrich the lives of the people. Our nation's shipping rights have been lost, industries have declined, and the people's livelihoods are withering. The construction of a shipping industry is truly a matter of utmost urgency. The late Premier Sun Yat-sen thoroughly reviewed global trends and deeply understood the major ailments within the country. With mature deliberation and meticulous planning, he included comprehensive elaborations of the path to shipping industry construction in the Three Principles of the People, the Nation-Building Program, the Industrial Plan, and other key documents for establishing the Party and the nation. He explicitly indicated the strategies, determined the methods, and repeatedly emphasized these points tirelessly. He provided us, his revolutionary comrades, with a perfect and precise blueprint. Therefore, for Party comrades today, in discussing shipping industry construction, our research and plans cannot surpass those of the late Premier. Besides following his teachings and the political program, there is no more convenient, better, or complete path. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is the largest and oldest shipping organization in our country and the sole foundation for the Party and the nation to revitalize shipping and save the nation in the future. How it should be managed is undoubtedly a matter that must adhere to the late Premier's instructions as a prerequisite. Therefore, the resolution of the Second Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee in June of last year to place it under the direct management of the National Government was indeed a diligent adherence to the late Premier's will. However, due to the unclearly defined boundaries between state and private enterprise, the situation has become increasingly entangled, leading to incessant disputes. Many proposals deviate from the Party's principles of consolidation, hindering progress. This has significant implications, potentially shaking the faith in our ideology and the implementation of our political program. I, Tieqiao, have been entrusted with government orders and have had the guidance and supervision to manage the company's affairs for over two years. I have upheld the mission of the Party and the nation, and I have examined the internal situation of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Based on two years of observation and experience, I believe that the most fundamental solution, the best strategy, is to follow the political program established by the late Premier and nationalize it. Only then can past disputes and difficulties be resolved, and future consolidation and development become attainable. The next best option, the alternative middle plan, is to emulate Japan's successful model of revitalizing its shipping industry by having the nation manage the Nippon Yusen Kaisha. Setting a period for national management can also prevent the corruption of shareholding cliques and their destructive influence, thereby achieving significant progress. If we abandon these top two strategies and choose a different path, it would lack a basis in both Party principles and precedents, leading us down a wrong road. Whether we choose to return it to private management or transform it into a joint public-private venture, our experiences in the past and our assessment of the current situation indicate that we would merely repeat past mistakes and fall into a dead end. This would undermine the Party and the nation's credibility and is undoubtedly a doomed, inferior strategy. The benefits and losses in this matter are as different as a hair's breadth and a thousand miles. As a Party member and fulfilling my duty, I dare not remain silent. I will now roughly explain the three strategies - the best, middle, and worst - for your consideration and deliberation. The Party and the nation's shipping industry depend on it.

(1) The Best Plan: Nationalization based on the Three Principles and the political program.

(A) Method: Based on the current situation of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, nationalization only requires the government's leadership and support by providing economic credit. It does not require raising a large amount of cash upfront, which would cause unnecessary doubts and hesitation.

(First) Methods for Compensating Share Capital can be divided into three types:

(A) Purchase entirely according to the current market price of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's shares. (Omission) The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company itself has the capacity to raise this amount without requiring the government to exert effort.

(B) Compensate according to the nominal value of all actual shares and newly issued shares (according to the new shipping shares and property shares issued by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company with remaining profits, totaling 4.4 million taels and 4.4 million yuan, which have not been formally approved by government authorities and have no legal basis). Shareholders would already benefit greatly from compensation at face value, but to show the Party's magnanimity, it can still be done. It can be guaranteed by using the customs tonnage dues collected from ship revenue as a guarantee fund, issuing shareholder bonds in installments with 3% interest, and expecting to clear it in fifteen years. Among this, the number of Sheng shares (i.e., 28,400 shipping shares and 14,200 property shares) should be further deducted. The actual amount only requires issuing public bonds of 8 million taels.

(C) To take an even more lenient step, compensate according to the calculated value of the property. Calculate the total property, after deducting debts, with a remaining amount of slightly over 20 million taels. It is proposed to issue public bonds with the aforementioned tonnage dues as a guarantee fund, extending the repayment period to twenty-five years. However, this method seems to be too disadvantageous for the government. According to the above three methods, whether repaying in cash or issuing public bonds, and with the public bonds having a guaranteed fund for interest, the bonds are reliable for purchase. This is vastly different from previously owning shares in name only, with no official dividends or interest. Shareholders will undoubtedly be willing to comply. The government only provides tonnage dues as a guarantee, and it only requires sixty to seventy million taels annually to be repaid in fifteen or twenty-five years. According to current gold standard tariffs, an additional 600,000 taels can be collected annually, which would not affect the national treasury in the slightest.

(Second) Raising Funds for Consolidation: The total funds required for consolidation are approximately 20 million yuan. Ten million yuan will be used to repay the large debt to HSBC, and ten million yuan will be taken from the total property for construction purposes such as shipbuilding and dock construction. The property withdrawn from HSBC will serve as collateral (valued at slightly over 30 million). Alternatively, the government can transfer the collateral to the Central Bank for mortgage or have it mortgaged by major domestic banks. With verified property, the banking syndicate will certainly accept it.

(Third) Organization of Personnel: Once nationalized, the organization of personnel should consider the execution, supervision, and oversight aspects. I believe that there should be one Director-General and seven Directors and seven Supervisors, all specially appointed by the National Government. The Directors should include representatives from the industrial and banking sectors, each responsible for design, innovation, and supervision. Three Standing Directors should be designated, and the Supervisors should be selected from among the Standing Directors, including representatives from the National Government's Auditing Department, Ministry of Communications, Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Industrial Bank, and shipping industry. The term of office for all personnel should be three years.

As for the reasons for this nationalization, from the Party's standpoint, all of our comrades are well aware. Secondly, it relates to national defense, military transportation, culture, industry, foreign trade, and other matters, all of which should be nationalized. Furthermore, the establishment and development of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company relied entirely on official capital and resources. The corruption and transformation to private management by greedy officials are also well-known facts. It should be nationalized without any doubt.

(2) The Middle Plan: National Management.

The policy of national management was already resolved by the Second Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee, so there is no need to reiterate the reasons. However, there are four prerequisites that must be confirmed by the Plenary Session to resolve the company's disputes and prevent destructive conflicts.

(First) The term of national management should be specified as fifteen years, so that national policies can be implemented according to the schedule and the managing personnel can achieve success within a set time. This is based on Japan's successful national management model of the Nippon Yusen Kaisha and is highly worthy of reference.

(Second) National management also requires debt restructuring and fund raising to have a hopeful future. The method is the same as raising funds for national consolidation, except that there is no need to repay the share capital. A portion of the tonnage dues can be reallocated as a fund for issuing consolidation bonds, making it more flexible.

(Third) The government should provide a guaranteed interest rate, which only costs three to four hundred thousand annually. This demonstrates the Party and the nation's sincerity in revitalizing shipping, reinforces shareholders' faith, and increases the fluidity of funds and the speed of consolidation. If there is a surplus, official dividends and bonuses will be formally distributed, then there will be no need for guaranteed interest. The government may only be nominally responsible for it or may not spend anything at all.

(Fourth) For the organization of national management personnel, I believe that the original proposal of the Second Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee can be maintained, with both committees and specialists working together. However, one person each from the industrial, banking, and shipping sectors should be added to the committee, one to promote industry and economic development through mutual coordination and another to achieve the effect of uncovering hidden issues through mutual supervision.

(3) The Worst Plan: Joint Public-Private Management and Returning to Private Management.

Joint public-private management is illogical and will inevitably fail. Firstly, if the government engages in joint management, it would be equivalent to repealing the provisions of the Party's political program, thereby losing the faith of the national masses in the Party's ideology. Secondly, the government emphasizes national policies, while businesses emphasize profitability, and their goals are fundamentally different, making cooperation difficult. Thirdly, with government and business in the same boat, there will be power struggles and mutual constraints. We are already suffering under this system, so how can we repeat the same mistake? Fourthly, with the main entity of government and business not clearly defined, external doubts will increase, and it will be difficult to establish credibility. With such conflicting phenomena everywhere, how can there be any possibility of mutual assistance? (Omission)

News on the Preparations for the National Silk Exhibition

Director Yang Came to Shanghai to Solicit Items

Preparatory Meeting to be Held Today

The National Products Exhibition Hall of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, to promote the sales of domestic silk, is preparing a National Domestic Silk Exhibition, scheduled to be held in the capital in mid-April. The director of the hall, Yang Duo, came to Shanghai in person the day before yesterday, in addition to dispatching staff to collect products from various regions, to discuss with the Shanghai Commercial Consolidation Association and the Commodity Exhibition Center, as well as the local silk trade association, to collect items separately, and decided to convene a preparatory meeting for the silk industry at the Shanghai Commercial Consolidation Association meeting room at 3 pm today (20th) to discuss the implementation method. It is reported that the content of the exhibition is divided into the following five parts: (1) Academic Research Department: displaying the achievements of various sericulture and textile schools and various improved silk venues for technical or industrial and commercial research, specimens or models of silkworm body reproduction and anatomy, pathological conditions of sericulture, and remedial methods and statistical diagrams and experiments, and various publications on sericulture and silk; (2) Machinery Department: displaying tools for silkworm raising, mulberry planting, silk reeling, silk weaving, and embroidery; (3) Sericulture Department: displaying various types of silkworm eggs, silkworm seeds, silkworm moths from various regions, and silkworm clothes and native mulberry varieties, improved mulberry varieties, etc.; (4) Silk Cocoon Department: displaying white silk, yellow silk, gray silk, foreign silk, factory silk, natural silk, broken silk, silk floss, silk thread, local silk, dry silk, silk spinning, silkworm spinning, fishing net silk, raw silk, silkworm silk, etc.; (5) Silk Weaving Department: displaying various kinds of silk fabrics, crepe, Ge fabric, gauze, silk, cotton velvet, Qi fabric, silk thread, spring spinning, silk pongee, silk velvet embroidery, and silk woven clothing supplies, etc.

Crew Members of the Flying Tiger Ship Describe the Circumstances of the Collision and Sinking

The accident of the Sanbei Flying Tiger Wheel has been repeatedly recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday, the crew members of the ship returned to Shanghai on the bureau's Chang'an Wheel, including the chief mate, Yan Zurui, and 44 others. When they met with reporters yesterday, they gave a very detailed account of the truth about the Flying Tiger accident. The following is a brief record:

Circumstances of the Collision: The Flying Tiger Wheel, the Yongxing Jiangxin, and the Jiangzhen warship were all docked at the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company wharf in Hankou. At noon on the 24th of last month, the Flying Tiger was ordered to move to the commercial port. During the turning of the ship, its stern compartment collided violently with the bow of the Jiangzhen warship. A large hole was immediately punched in the stern of the Flying Tiger, and the river water rushed in, making it impossible to save. Therefore, the ship sank in only twenty minutes.

Boatmen Seize Property: There were small sampans in the river. When the Flying Tiger had an accident, forty or fifty small sampans, under the pretext of rescue, swarmed onto the ship. They used axes to chop open the doors of the cabins where the crew members and sailors lived, and then entered to rob. They looted all public and private items, crew members' luggage, money, etc., seeing everything they could grab. Several sailors stepped forward to try to take it back, but when they refused to let them enter the room, the sampan men used axes to chop at them. Two sailors were injured on the spot. There were no water police present at the time, so they had to be robbed clean. The crew members' personal belongings alone suffered losses of nearly 10,000 yuan. Everyone barely escaped with their lives.

Ship Damage: The Flying Tiger Wheel sank completely at 12 o'clock that night, leaving only the chimney. The total loss reached more than 200,000 yuan. The company is currently planning to salvage it, but it is said that the salvage fee is extremely high, so work has not yet begun.

Negotiations in Progress: After the Flying Tiger accident, Sanbei Company reported it to the insurance company. It is now heard that the insurance company said that this ship was sunk by a warship, which does not comply with ordinary insurance regulations, and there is news that it will not be compensated. The company has now submitted a report to the headquarters, detailing that the collision was the fault of the warship and requesting the Navy Department to recognize and compensate for the loss.

Shipping News

New Taikoo Ship Coming: To expand its coastal shipping business in China, British Taikoo Company specially built the Taiyuan and Jinan wheels. The Taiyuan wheel has been completed first and has been assigned to run on the Shanghai-Guangdong line. The Jinan new wheel, which was built in the company's Hong Kong factory, has also been completed. With a load of more than 3,000 tons, it is scheduled to open its maiden voyage to Shanghai on the 23rd of this month, and it will also be ordered to run the Nanyang class. After the completion of these two ships, the company has a total of 71 large and small sea-going ships, totaling 165,000 net tons.

Chichibu and Ryuta Start Classes: The second ship Shichibu Maru and the third ship Ryuda Maru of the three Pacific Ocean giants built by the Japanese Post Office have been completed and the passenger seats have also been installed. The style is the same as that of Asami Maru. Chichibu is scheduled to start the first class on April 1st, and Asami is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on April 18th.

Record of the Annual Meeting of the Waiming Chamber of Commerce

Criticism of Current Affairs in Our Country

Electing the President and Directors

The Waiming Chamber of Commerce, composed of foreign firms in this port, held its annual meeting the other day. President Laiman was unable to attend due to illness, and Vice President Mr. McMeekan presided over the meeting. He reported on the chamber's work over the past year, briefly stating that the radio signal station established by the Chinese government on North Saddle Island has been established for several months and has benefited shipping greatly. If the experiment is effective, it is also planned to add another one somewhere in the future so that ships passing the Amherst Reef will not encounter danger even in fog. He then said that the ambassadors of various countries to China recently negotiated with the Chinese authorities on the agreement on the Shanghai Provisional Court without consulting the Public Works Bureau and foreign firms in Shanghai. This kind of arbitrary action is very disappointing. He then said that the sharp drop in silver prices has greatly harmed foreign firms engaged in the import trade, especially the weaving industry. Recently, the Chamber of Commerce has discussed setting up a piece goods association to stipulate the standard for trading in Shanghai's general yuan currency as one of its main purposes, which has been approved by chambers of commerce in various countries. After passing the account briefly, Mr. McMeekan and Mr. Saito were elected as the president and vice president of this year, and 12 new directors including Poolson were elected and the meeting adjourned.

Jade Import Tax Rate Reduced

The Municipal Commercial Consolidation Association received an approval order from the Ministry of Finance yesterday regarding the reduction of import taxes on jade, and specially sent a letter to notify the two jade industry groups. The original letter said, "We are writing to inform you that we have received a letter stating that the increase in import taxes on rough jade has affected business, please review and reduce the amount. We have presented the matter to the Ministry of Industry, Commerce and Finance, and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has issued an order stating that the case has been reviewed and noted. On March 17, we received the Ministry of Finance's Order Guan Zi No. 993, stating, "We have learned of the matter. We have investigated the request to reduce the import tax rate on rough jade. According to the Guangzhou General Chamber of Commerce, the raw materials of jade are made into utensils in Guangdong Province and are still sold overseas. Not only are there more impurities and waste when they are made, but before they are dissected, their true value is difficult to determine, which is not the same as agate and gemstones that have not been polished and retain their valuable properties. Therefore, this item of rough jade should be classified in the current tax rules. Item No. 718, not listed, is taxed at 35% of the value to maintain craftsmanship." In addition to the instructions, we have also ordered the Customs Service to order the General Customs Office to order all customs offices to comply. We are sending this letter to you accordingly and hope that you will check and comply. This is addressed to Shen Pu Jade Bang Kun He Tang Guang Yun Jade Bang Kun Yu Tang."

Local News 2

Zhou Zenyi Escapes Kidnapping

Athlete Uses Fists to Repel Bandits

Hawker Suffers Innocent Disaster, Zhou Also Injured in Thigh

Police Arrive in Response to Alarm

Bandits Flee Empty-Handed

Zhou Fujiou, a wealthy merchant from the old Jiangxi, started his career in the salt industry and is well-known in Shanghai. His three sons, Zitain, inherited the legacy of their ancestors and associated with many wealthy merchants. In the past, he built his own residence at No. 1 Xiaoshadu Road and had a good reputation in the business community. However, in recent years, he moved to No. 672 Jing'an Lane, Jing'an Temple Road. Zitain had four sons, and Zenyi is the eldest. At the age of 19, he studied at the Shanghai Municipal Council's Gezhi Public School on Beihai Road. He is tall and sturdy, has the appearance of a martial artist, and is fond of sports and ball games. He is proficient in kicking and striking, so he is praised by his classmates in the school. Yesterday afternoon, he suddenly encountered bandits outside the school gate who intended to kidnap him. Fortunately, he relied on his agile skills to avoid a major disaster. There were three bandits in total. They first rented a car No. 17532 from Jiujiang Automobile Company on Jiujiang Road and waited outside the school for two hours. At about 5:10 pm, Zhou Zenyi went out with three or four classmates. Before they had walked ten steps, the bandits greeted them and demanded that they get in the car. Zhou took advantage of the bandits' unpreparedness to repel the enemy with his fists. In the rush, a gunshot was fired, injuring a hawker. He immediately ran back to school. The bandits were unwilling to give up and fired another shot, hitting his left thigh. He entered the gate injured and told the principal. The bandits also took the opportunity to drive away. Zhou was fortunate to avoid this disaster when the bandits were already close.

Using Fists to Repel Bandits: Zhou Zenyi went out of the school gate with two friends at about 5:10 pm, which was long after the class was over. He had finished playing ball games with his friends. The bandits had been waiting on the road for a long time. When they saw Zhou coming, two bandits greeted him on the road. When they were close to him, they showed him their guns and ordered him not to move. Zhou's friends had already walked several steps ahead, so he was isolated and unable to call for help. One bandit held him in his hand, gradually rising from below, intending to point at Zhou's chest and force him into the car. However, Zhou suddenly came up with a clever idea in his extreme fear, signaling to the two bandits that he would obey, and in an instant, he suddenly waved his arm and punched the bandit's arm straight. The bandit retreated in pain and still held his gun firmly, staggering backwards.

Hawker Injured by Bullet: Although the bandit retreated, he still held the pistol in his hand. He immediately pulled the trigger and fired in the direction of where Zhou was standing. Zhou Zenyi, before he could catch his breath, saw the muzzle of the gun pointing at him and knew that things were not good, so he bowed his body to dodge. The bullet went off to the side and hit the right arm of Zhu Xicai, a hawker diagonally opposite the school gate. Zhou immediately turned around and ran wildly towards the school gate in the smoke. Fortunately, the place was not far away, and he arrived in an instant. The injured hawker was later sent to Renji Hospital for treatment by the police.

Shot in the Thigh: Zhou Zenyi ran back to school with great speed, waving his arms and moving his thighs, which was the result of practicing racing in sports. However, the bandits saw the fat meat that seemed to be in their mouths, but lost it again, and were immediately disgusted. They fired a shot at him. A bullet flew and hit Zhou's left thigh. When he entered the gate with his injuries, the police had already gathered in response to the alarm and were chasing the bandits with whistles. The bandits took advantage of the commotion to drive back in the original car. Zhou Zenyi told Deputy Director Zeng Xiaojun what he had encountered and was immediately sent to Baolong Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the injury was not critical. After applying the medicine, he immediately went out and was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment by his family in a car.

Bandits Rent a Car: Afterwards, someone reported to the Laoza Police Station that the license plate number of the bandits' car was White Plate 17532. This car belonged to Jiujiang Automobile Company on Jiujiang Road. At about 2:40 pm yesterday, a young customer with a mustache came to rent it. The driver was Chen Luosheng. The car was a Panqi sedan. The license plate number was Concession 17532 and Chinese Area 4218. The car went out of the gate and first went to the New World Company to wait briefly, picked up two customers, and then drove to Beihai Road to wait. After the incident, the driver Chen Luosheng saw that the situation was not good and jumped out. The bandits drove away. Later in the evening, the car was found near Xiaoshadu in western Shanghai and was not damaged.

A Thief Shot Dead in Front of Boyong Hospital Last Night

Robbery at a Yunnan Road Native Goods Store

A Robbery also Occurred on Avenue Edward VII

The Two Cases Happened About Ten Minutes Apart

Shanghai Teeming with Bandits

Last night at 8:40 PM, four bandits, dressed in blue cloth shirts and trousers and speaking with local accents, suddenly entered the Sheng Dingchang Native Goods Store, No. 601-602 Yunnan Road, owned by Sheng Huaiyu from Suzhou. Two bandits, one with a gun, stood guard at the door, while another stood in front of the counter to watch. The two bandits who were empty-handed jumped into the store and robbed about four hundred and forty-odd yuan in cash from the counter. They then carried the stolen goods and fled towards the second alley of Yudeli across the street and north, disappearing without a trace. The owner immediately reported the loss to the police station, requesting an investigation. However, before even ten minutes had passed, another robbery occurred at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Tibet Road. One thief was immediately pursued and caught by patrol officers and shot dead in front of Boyong Hospital. This led to the mistaken belief that it was the same incident as the store robbery. Upon further investigation, it was found that they were two separate cases.

Diamond Ring Robbed: Last night around 8:30 PM, a certain Mr. A, of advanced age and dressed in fine clothes, was wearing a diamond ring on his hand. He was suddenly stopped by three or more thugs on the western section of Avenue Edward VII. The diamond ring was robbed, and twenty-seven yuan in silver in his pocket was also taken. The robbers then fled. Afterwards, the victim followed the robbers, tailing them to the Yunnan Road intersection opposite the Great World. He reported to the police post, saying that the person in the black shirt ahead was not a good person. The police, upon receiving the information, immediately drew their guns and gave chase.

Ten Shots Fired: A detective from the Old North Gate Police Station also joined the pursuit. The robbers, seeing the police, resisted with their guns. The police opened fire, firing about ten shots in total. The robbers were no match and were hit four times, falling to the ground and dying. The deceased was about twenty-four or twenty-five years old, wearing a black Chinese silk gown. The original stolen diamond ring was found in his pocket, but the silver coins were gone.

All Perpetrators in the Stepmother Slaying Case Requested to be Sentenced to Death by the Police

Chen Hengcai is of Short Stature

The Lawyer Asked How Could He Commit Murder

Closing Arguments Were Declared Yesterday

Sentencing Scheduled for the 28th

The case of Zhang Wenqing from Huzhou, along with her lover Chen Hengcai, conspiring with Yao Yonggui and Gao Jintang to kill the stepmother Zhang Su, continued in the Second Provisional Court yesterday morning for closing arguments. The audience of men and women was as crowded as in previous sessions, indicating the public's great interest in this case. First, the lawyer for the victim's family presented the settlement agreement from the previous lawsuit between Zhang Wenqing's legal mother, Zhang Su, and the concubine Zhang Su regarding the management of the late husband Zhang Fusheng's property. Judge Ren Ji reviewed the document and then handed it to Zhang Wenqing to read. According to Zhang Wenqing, the written amount of seven thousand taels of silver was actually a mistake for eight thousand four hundred taels, and she was not present when the document was written. Next, lawyer Fan Gang defended Chen Hengcai, arguing that Chen was accused of conspiring with the other defendants. He asked the court to consider Chen's short stature and lack of knowledge, asking how could he conspire to commit murder. Furthermore, the testimonies of the defendants were full of contradictions. Yao Yonggui testified that Chen invited him to fight and intimidate the deceased, but Yao and Gao acted impulsively and killed the person. Chen was acting on his master's orders and should not be considered a co-conspirator. He should be treated leniently. Next, Gao Jintang's lawyer defended Gao, saying that Gao did not know the Zhang family and had no animosity towards them. He was merely being used as a tool. The police's charge of Article 284 against Gao was too severe and should be treated leniently. Zhang Wenqing's lawyer, Wang Fushang, also offered supplementary arguments, stating that Zhang's confession at the police station may have been coerced and should not be adopted. Furthermore, the murder weapon could not be proven to have been given by Zhang. Although the Zhang family had lost a knife, it was questionable whether the knife wounds on the deceased were inflicted by that knife. The missing knife from the Zhang family had not been found. Finally, the police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, rebutted each point made by Wang, saying that this case was unprecedented. The four defendants had premeditated and committed the crime together and should be sentenced to death to serve as a warning to others. At this point, the arguments from all sides concluded. Judge Luo announced that sentencing would be on the morning of March 28th, and the defendants were returned to custody.

Trial Opens for Sun Xunqu's Married Daughter's Property Dispute

Sun's Inheritance Already Divided Twice

Sun Zhongyao Emits a Sigh in Court

The Distribution of Property in the Fourteenth Year Was Not Formal

Plaintiff Jinghua Was Absent from Court Yesterday

After the death of Sun Xunqu, a wealthy businessman from Wuxi, his estate of over 500,000 yuan was divided into six shares by his sons Sun Zhongwei, Zhongyao, Zhongying, Zhongchu, Zhonghu, and Zhongju several years ago. Sun also had two daughters, the eldest named Jinghua, who married Hu Disheng. Recently, Jinghua cited the 181st resolution of the Central Executive Committee and the declaration of the Second National Congress, stating that women, whether married or unmarried, have the right to inherit property. She hired lawyer Song Mingxun and filed a lawsuit against Zhongwei et al. in the Provisional Court, requesting that the estate be divided into eight shares so that her sister could also receive a share. A summary of her complaint has already been published in the newspapers. The case was heard yesterday afternoon by Judge Feng Shide in the Tenth Court. The plaintiff, Hu Sun Jinghua, was absent and represented by lawyer Song. According to the lawyer, the defendants stated that the property was divided in 1925, but this was not accurate. The defendants divided the estate in March 1928. The agreement stated that all real estate was distributed according to the will. The will conflicts with current laws and is therefore invalid. Furthermore, it is questionable whether this will is genuine. Therefore, he requested that the property be divided according to the law. The defendants Zhongwei, Zhongyao, and Zhongying, accompanied by their lawyers, Wang Fushang et al., appeared in court. The others were absent and had no legal representation. Sun Zhongwei testified that he was 48 years old. His father's estate was indeed divided in 1925, and there was a will as proof. In February 1928, the estate was re-divided because the younger brothers were young, and their shares were managed by the elders. The shares of myself, Zhongyao, and Zhongying were kept in the Shanghai Industrial Bank's vault and could only be withdrawn with the joint signatures of the depositors. If the court wanted to inspect the deeds of the property, they could be produced next time. Lawyer Wang Fushang stated that the defendants divided the property once in 1925 and again in 1928. The plaintiff requested a re-division, but it was unclear which distribution she was referring to. Lawyer Song replied that since the division agreement mentioned distribution according to the will, Xunqu must have already passed away at the time of the distribution. Therefore, the plaintiff was referring to the 1928 distribution. The agreement also stated that the family division was strictly according to the will and equally divided, meaning each person received one share. Defendant Sun Zhongyao, a 29-year-old accountant, testified that the plaintiff was his older sister and that the estate was actually divided in 1925. The lawyer for defendant Zhongying stated that Zhongying had been adopted into the eldest branch, Wangjiao Gong, and the inheritance he received was from Wangjiao Gong, not from Xunqu. Therefore, Zhongying should not be listed as a defendant in this case. Zhongying testified that Wangjiao Gong had a large estate, which Xunqu managed on his behalf after Wangjiao died early. After Xunqu passed away, Wangjiao's branch was inherited by me, but his estate was not entirely mine. What I received was one-sixth of the combined property of Wang and Xunqu, which was far from what I should have received. I did not value the estate and did not object at the time. Now, I am being sued. If I had known there would be a lawsuit, I would have insisted on taking sole possession of Wangjiao's estate so that I would not be involved today. His words expressed a sense of regret. Witness Hu Disheng testified that the distribution did occur in 1928, and he was present at the time. The distribution in 1925 was not formal. Judge Feng ordered both parties to withdraw and adjourned the hearing.

The Thieves Had Leisurely Interests

The Robbers of the Four Banks' Reserve

Watched a Soccer Match at the Baseball Field

Six Men and Women Arrested on the Spot

2,000 Yuan in Stolen Goods Recovered from the Thieves' Den

The reserve of the four banks, namely, China & South Sea Bank, Yieh Commercial Bank, The Continental Bank, and Jincheng Bank, sent an old clerk to deliver banknotes and coins worth 46,000 yuan accompanied by armed police escorts, at 2:00 pm on the 13th of this month, to the banks on the Bund, such as, The Chartered Bank of India, Australia and China and The Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation, when passing Guangdong Road, they were robbed by bandits wielding weapons. First the armed police were disarmed, then the bank notes and coins were robbed and they escaped in a car. The next day, the car was found in the city. The car owner was ordered to take it back and the police were ordered to arrest the fleeing robbers. It was already in the previous newspapers. It wasn't until the day before yesterday that Liang Chengyu, a private detective of the Old North Gate Police Station, received a report that the robbers in this case were hiding at the baseball field on Observatory Road in the French Concession. Detective Liang, along with detectives Feng Zhiming and Heden, and detectives from the French Concession Police Station, rushed to the baseball field at 3:00 pm. At that time, Jinan and Huale were holding a soccer championship match. Six robbers, Yuan Genfa, Yu Ziyi, Qian Amao, Xia Zhanchun, from Suzhou and women Li Wang and Zhou MeiMei, were arrested from the audience and taken back to the police station. After investigation, it was learned that accomplices were living at No. 54 Mintini Road. When they went to arrest them again, but they had already fled after hearing the news. Only the original stolen goods of 2,000 yuan in banknotes and silver were seized in the robbers' den. Yesterday morning, the six men and women, including Yuan, were taken to the First Provisional Court, where Judge Gao Junxiang interrogated them. Detective Liang reported the situation of the arrest, and said that Li Wang was Yuan Genfa's mistress and Zhou MeiMei was Xia Zhanchun's lover. When the robbery was carried out, there were two women in the car that the robbers were traveling in, or the robbers were using women to avoid being arrested and checked along the way. Now it is still necessary to investigate in detail and request an extension of 14 days. Lawyer Fan Gang, lawyer for defendant Yuan Genfa, and Lawyer Ye Fukan, lawyer for Qian Amao and Zhou MeiMei, cross-examined Detective Liang. Yuan, Yu, Qian, and Xia, four defendants, all confessed that they opened a brothel in the French Concession. They firmly denied the robbery case. Li Wang confessed that her husband's name was Li Genrong, not Yuan. Zhou MeiMei confessed that she was 19 years old and lived at No. 45 Baoyu Lane and did not know any of the defendants. Judge Gao ordered the defendants to be detained separately and adjourned the hearing.

A Rickshaw Puller Raped a Nine-Year-Old Girl

This is an Inhumane Act

One Can Sigh at the Declining Morality of Society

Zhang Afu, a native of Qingjiang, 36 years old, who lives in the overpass building of Linqing Lane, Jiangwan Road, Zhabei, is in charge of managing the alley. His wife, Chen, 30 years old, has a daughter named Xiaomei, who is only nine years old and is very intelligent. Zhang adores her like a pearl. Yesterday morning, Zhang went out for business, and his wife went out to buy vegetables, leaving only Xiaomei alone to guard the house. Ma Afu, 24 years old, from Tongzhou, who used to pull rickshaws and lives at No. 30 of the alley, (his wife, Wang, is working outside,) broke into the house and, seeing that there was no one in the room, began to play with her. Xiaomei was very innocent, and since Ma was also acquainted with her, she stayed by Ma's side and did not leave. Who knew that Ma would suddenly become animalistic and have lustful thoughts. He pushed Xiaomei to the ground, took off her pants, and raped her. Xiaomei was young and weak and could not resist, allowing him to ravage her, causing serious injuries to her lower body, with blood flowing all over the ground, and the pain was unbearable. Ma, seeing that his wish had been fulfilled, was about to escape, but Chen happened to return and, seeing this situation, was filled with uncontrollable anger. She called her husband together and led her daughter to twist Ma to the Fifth District Headquarters. The director believed that Ma's rape of a young girl was extremely illegal, and he observed that the girl's wounds were quite severe and she could not walk, so he sentenced her to the judicial department for strict investigation.

Mrs. Wei Zhang, wife of Wei Jia-nian, residing at No. 4, Fu'an Lane, Caiyang Wharf, Nanshi, aged thirty-eight, suddenly quarreled yesterday because her thirteen-year-old son was beaten by Ji Tianrong, a leather craftsman living nearby. Child Playing Dangerously on the Platform

A Ball Rolls onto the Tracks

Two Feet Crushed by a Train

At the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway station platform, a child named Hu Houquan, aged ten, was playing with a ball yesterday afternoon around 3:00 PM when the ball suddenly rolled onto the tracks below. Hu, eager to retrieve the ball, went down to the tracks. At that moment, a train came speeding by, and Hu was unable to avoid it in time. Both of his feet were crushed. Bleeding profusely, he lost consciousness. Railway workers arrived and carried him to Renji Hospital for treatment.

Yesterday at 1:00 PM, a man surnamed Jia, a countryman in his thirties, resembling a laborer, was walking past the front of No. 387, Min'guo Road, French Concession, east of the Baptist Church, when he suddenly collapsed and died. Lake Chow Chamber of Commerce Plans Reorganization

Wang Yiting Has Not Yet Convened a Meeting

The Lake Chow Chamber of Commerce has not held a meeting for six years. The previous directors have long been out of date. The Social Affairs Bureau appointed Wang Yiting and seven others as reorganization committee members, designating Wang as chairman to convene meetings. It is reported that all committee members have received official letters of appointment from the Social Affairs Bureau. Chen Aishi, Yang Kuihou, Zhu Bangsheng, and Shen Tianxin, four committee members, jointly sent a letter to Chairman Wang, requesting that he convene a meeting as soon as possible to comply with the order. Wang Yiting replied, stating that he had received the official letter and understood. The charter of the Lake Chow Chamber of Commerce does not comply with current regulations, and the qualifications of the directors are outdated. Former directors stated that the chamber has been occupied by troops for a long time, making it impossible to hold meetings, elect new members, or revise the charter. A previous notice was issued to convene at the Cocoon Industry Association, but the Social Affairs Bureau stopped the meeting that day, and it was not successful. The former directors may not agree to the reorganization. It is proposed that the Social Affairs Bureau draft the charter, which Director Pan has agreed to do. It is expected to be issued within a few days. Once the charter is received, the chamber can hold a meeting. The temporary reorganization can be delayed to avoid misunderstandings among the townspeople. However, it is reported that the Social Affairs Bureau will strictly order the former directors of the chamber, who were elected six years ago, to hand over control to the reorganization committee to facilitate the reorganization, and will not allow them to delay any further.

Bureau of Visits Promotes Bamboo Carving

Personnel Sent to Fenghua First, Then to Jiading for Investigation

The Bureau of Visits of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce believes that the bamboo carvings of Jiading are excellent in production and have a long-standing reputation. They are highly artistic. Not only do Chinese people like to buy and use them, but foreigners also treasure them. Therefore, these utensils are exported overseas every year. However, this industry has recently been declining, resulting in sluggish sales. Although Fenghua, Zhejiang, also produces bamboo carvings, the production is slightly inferior, and sales are also not strong. In order to promote the industry, the Bureau of Visits has sent staff member Yang Zhuojun to Fenghua first to investigate. After completion, he will go to Jiading for investigation in order to design promotion plans. It is reported that Mr. Yang, after receiving the order, has scheduled to take a boat to Ningbo and then to Fenghua tomorrow (the 21st) to conduct an investigation with the local Construction Bureau on the latest situation of the industry.

Record of the Public Banquet of Representatives of Public Organizations in Wusong

Requesting Various Agencies to Protect Merchant Ships

Zheng Shushan, Chairman of the Wusong Chamber of Commerce, Lu Damin, representative of shipping merchants from Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and others held a public banquet yesterday afternoon at the Ningbo Merchant Fire Brigade building on Wusong Outer Ma Road, honoring Tax Commissioner Yang and representatives from various agencies. They also presented them with plaques and silver articles in recognition of their virtuous governance. Among those present were Deng Zhenquan, Commander of the Wusong Fortress, Wu Zhennan, Director of the National River Patrol, Jiang Bin, Naval Commander, Zhu Bingzheng, Chief of the Fourth District of Water Police, Chen Youhua, Chief of the Seventh District of Water Police, Chief Zhang of the Seventh District, First Division, Team Leader Wu of the Salt Smuggling Bureau, Wu Jia, Magistrate of Baoshan County, Shen Jing, Police Chief of the Public Security Bureau, Shen Fusheng, Director of the Shipping Bureau, and Tang Zuanzhi, Commander of the Security Corps. First, Zheng Shushan, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, delivered a eulogy, followed by a response from Tax Commissioner Yang. Then, a joint meeting was held, during which Chairman Zheng proposed that the fishing season is approaching, and there will be more ships traveling to and fro. However, piracy is rampant, making shipowners fearful. If strict defense is not implemented, there will be three negative consequences: (1) National tax revenue cannot be fully collected; (2) The livelihood of shipowners depends entirely on the income from the fishing season; (3) The prosperity or decline of Wusong's commerce depends on the number of ships arriving at Wusong. Therefore, it is requested that the Coastal Patrol, the Naval Command, and the Fourth District of Water Police jointly dispatch warships for strict patrols to ensure public safety and increase revenue. In case of emergencies, it is requested that the fortress command pay special attention to the various sailing ships and be especially accommodating, as sailing ships must travel with the wind and tide. If they are prevented from entering the port during evening high tide due to martial law, and are subsequently attacked by bandits, it would be a death sentence. It is hoped that the military and police authorities will show understanding and provide protection. After deliberation, the authorities agreed to take responsibility and order their subordinates to comply. Chairman Zheng further stated that ships entering the Yangtze River have traditionally paid taxes according to regulations at the Fishing Boat Bureau, and the Customs had no tax collection relationship. Now, detailed inspections are being imposed, which inevitably delays time and causes losses. Therefore, he requested Tax Commissioner Yang to show understanding and order that the previous procedures be followed without causing difficulties. With just a few words, the shipowners received real benefits and invisible convenience, which is truly significant. Furthermore, the transportation of coal and charcoal is done by small cargo ships from the Yangtze River to supply the residents of the town. Although violations of the cargo handling procedures should be punished according to regulations, he hopes that Tax Commissioner Yang will consider their initial ignorance and grant leniency. People are not plants or trees, how can they not be grateful? In the past, the Customs sovereignty belonged to foreign management, and customs officials often extorted, delayed, levied arbitrary fines, and accepted bribes to release ships. Such abuses were ignored. Tax Commissioner Yang is well aware of these malpractices and seeks to eliminate them completely, so that state revenue will increase, and the people's hardships will be alleviated. The benefits received by the merchant ships are beyond description. The banquet and presentation of the plaques are not meant as repayment, but merely to express our gratitude and serve as a lasting memorial. After the discussions, the banquet began and everyone enjoyed themselves before dispersing.

Record of the Meeting of the Chinese and Foreign Charity Association

The Chinese and Foreign Charity Association held a board meeting at 5:00 PM on the 18th. The Chinese and foreign general secretaries reported on the charity work carried out, stating that since last year, grain funds had been released to Shaanxi, Gansu, Henan, Shandong, Shanxi, Hebei, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang provinces, totaling 381,923.88 silver dollars. This year, another 74,500 silver dollars have been allocated to Henan, Shaanxi, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang provinces for disaster relief. It was reported that Shaanxi has poor transportation, a complete lack of food, and the disaster victims' livelihoods have been cut off. Over two million people have died of starvation, and over 500,000 have fled the famine. It was decided to quickly allocate another 16,000 silver dollars. Next, Gansu, including Gaolan, Yuzhong, Dingxi, Tongwei, and Hongshui counties, has not received rain or snow since last autumn. Taohe, Lintao, Hezheng, Ningding, Yongjing, Wushan, Longxi, Taomin and other counties have been plagued by bandits, resulting in widespread displacement. There is no seed grain. It was decided to allocate another 10,000 silver dollars to provide assistance. Additionally, the previous 5,000 silver dollars for disaster relief in Yancheng, Jiangsu, and 4,000 silver dollars each for Xinghua, Funing, and Baoying were insufficient. The situation is dire, with starvation widespread and people waiting for death. Baoying is particularly severe, with the eastern townships being the hardest hit. Over 1,600 villages need urgent relief, and another 1,000 villages are in serious condition. Disaster victims are eating wild grass and wheat bran to survive, and many are unable to walk and are on the verge of death. If they are not rescued quickly, they will all starve to death. However, the disaster area is too wide and funding is difficult. It was decided to raise 10,000 silver dollars and allocate an additional 2,000 silver dollars each to Yancheng, Funing, and Xinghua, actually needing 4,000 silver dollars each, to alleviate the spring famine. It was also reported that western Henan has suffered repeated disasters, and northern Anhui has suffered repeated droughts, affecting as many as 21 counties. In addition, northern Jiangsu has suffered from consecutive years of famine, with no harvests. The people are in imminent danger of starvation. It was decided that unless donations are solicited from all sectors of society, it will be impossible to save these remaining people.

Anti-Opium Society Announces Statistics on Opium and Morphine Offenders in Jilin Province

Over 12,000 People Detained and Imprisoned in Three Years

The Chinese National Anti-Opium Society has been collecting various anti-opium achievements for years, and the materials are very comprehensive. Reports have been received successively from Jianghai Customs, national courts, and provincial and county governments. Apart from Jianghai Customs, which has submitted complete lists, national courts have submitted 70% and county governments 20%. All materials have been sorted and will be statistically released by the society's statistics department as a reference for future anti-opium measures. Among the reports, the most detailed are from the civil affairs departments of Zhejiang and Shanxi provinces, which have seriously handled this matter and obtained complete reports. The reports from Jilin province are also relatively concrete, as the provincial government and the High Court pay close attention to opium prohibition. Therefore, the reports from the counties under the province are also more detailed. The total number of opium and morphine offenders detained and imprisoned by courts and county governments, prisons, and detention centers in Jilin province in the three years of the Republic of China's 15th, 16th, and 17th years has been reported by the relevant authorities and compiled by the High Court and Civil Affairs Department, and has been analyzed and statistically completed by the Anti-Opium Society's statistics department. The total number of opium and morphine offenders detained and imprisoned in three prisons, eight courts, and twenty-five county prisons or detention centers in the three years of the Republic of China's 15th, 16th, and 17th years is 12,303, of which 10,407 are opium offenders, accounting for 84.6% of the total, and 1,896 are morphine offenders, accounting for 25.4% of the total. National Goods Factory Association Concerned About Donations in Zhejiang Province

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Association telegraphed Qian, Director of the Zhejiang Finance Department, stating that the purpose of machine-made imitations of foreign goods is to benefit the people and prevent leakage of wealth. In order to encourage industry and recover rights and interests, the government has issued orders to exempt them from donations to encourage them. The Zhejiang, Hangzhou, Ningbo, Shaoxing, Jinhua, Quzhou and Yan Prefectures, foreign cloth, woolen and down donation headquarters collect taxes and levies on machine-made imitations of woven products equal to those on foreign goods, and cause many difficulties. This prevents these woven goods from being sold extensively in Zhejiang Province, which is contrary to the government's intention to promote national goods. It is reported that the headquarters is contracted by a small number of merchants. The term will expire at the end of April this year. It is not known whether there will be open bidding, what the security deposit will be, and how much the annual contracted amount will be. It is requested that details be provided. It is proposed that relevant factories pool funds to bid, which will not affect the department's revenue, and will enable national goods to be sold as much as possible, avoiding long-term monopolies, which is the best of both worlds. This is specially telegraphed for consideration, and a reply is eagerly awaited.

Records of Meetings of Various Trade Associations

Charcoal Industry　On the morning of March 19th at 9:00 AM, the Charcoal Industry Guild convened a temporary industry conference with 35 industry representatives attending. Ye Zuojin and Wang Yunzhang went to the bureau to answer the questions. Zhu Shunlin and others from the Wushan boat gang were also present, claiming that the current 98% deduction was not good and that the footing was dark. Chen, a clerk, refuted this, saying that today's questioning was for the current 98% deduction. If there was anything wrong with the footing, it should have been done beforehand. It is proposed to submit it to the general membership meeting for discussion and appropriate measures. It was decided to pass the motion. After the discussion, a dinner party was held and the meeting adjourned.

Flowers and Trees Industry　The Flowers and Trees Industry Association has been preparing for a year, but because the procedures are not complete, on the 11th of this month, Huang Yueyuan and 19 others were re-appointed to continue the preparations. On the 18th, the second first preparatory committee meeting was held, chaired by Huang Yueyuan. (1) Meeting held as planned, (2) Chairman's report, (3) Assignment of duties. As a result, Huang Yueyuan was Chairman of the Standing Committee and Director of the General Affairs Department, Xi Zaixian was Finance Committee member, Shen Linyuan was Registration Committee member, Gao Fengshan was Investigation Committee member, Lu Mingzhao was Director of Affairs, (4) Passed eight assistant workers including Hong Songjiong, (5) Appointed Secretary Zhu Chuansheng. Meeting Adjourned.

Labor Union News

Pharmaceutical Industry Workers' Union　Yesterday's Executive Committee held a joint meeting, chaired by Sang Yutang, who performed the ceremony. (A) Chairman's report (B) Discussion (1) According to the letter from the members requesting an increase in wages and amendment of conditions, how to handle the case. It was resolved that the group leaders should refer to the original conditions, and if they are inappropriate, they should submit a written statement for review. (2) The group leaders should be responsible for reporting the general situation of the members of each industry and the deception of the capitalists so that they can be adopted. The resolution was passed. (3) The group leaders must at any time report the employment of non-industry personnel by the capitalists of each industry. The resolution was passed. (4) How should Kong Bingheng, a non-industry personnel employed by Hengli Pharmacy, be dealt with? It was resolved to inform the manager of the company to dismiss him. (5) Notify the Industrial Association and instruct the managers of each company that they must not employ non-industry personnel to serve as assistants in the future. The resolution was passed. (6) Conduct a thorough investigation of whether each company employs non-industry personnel to work. It was resolved that the group leaders should be responsible for the investigation. (7) The bylaws of the Industrial Association are inconsistent, how should they be expressed? It was resolved to submit the petition to the superior and determine that workers must absolutely organize a labor union. (8) (Omitted) (9) Determine the date of the Executive Committee's joint meeting. It was resolved to convene the meeting once a month and scheduled it for Wednesdays. (C) Temporary Motions (1) Comrade Zhao Riyuan proposed that Mao Yixing Honey Candy should be allowed to join the association. The resolution was rejected. (D) Meeting Adjourned.

He Xing Shipyard Labor Union　After the 6th re-election on March 11, the first meeting of the Executive Committee was held on the 18th with seven committee members present. Chairman Sheng Ade performed the ceremony and discussed the case. (1) The case of the assignment of duties was resolved. Shen Hongbin was elected as the standing committee, Zhou Qiaosheng as the general affairs, Wu Laibao as the organization, Qian Rengen as the publicity, and Yu Guifu as the training. (2) The proposal to subsidize the standing committee members' travel expenses was approved to subsidize four silver dollars per month. (3) The date for the regular meeting was scheduled and resolved to hold it every ten days. (4) The proposal to re-elect the group leader as soon as possible was approved. The meeting was adjourned after the discussion.

Weather Report

The weather forecast from the Xujiahui Observatory at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the low pressure formed in eastern Taiwan will move to the Ryukyus. The sky will be cloudy and slightly sunny. There is a cyclone around the Ryukyus. There is a slight wind in the coastal area of ​​China, with no direction and occasional light fog. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 53.2 and the lowest was 42.8. On the same day last year, the highest was 59.4 and the lowest was 35.8.

Theater News

The New New Garden Presents the Eighth Volume of Empress Dowager Cixi: The New New Garden on Nanjing Road declares that since its Zhong She Kun Qian Drama Troupe began staging the entire series of Empress Dowager Cixi, every performance has been sold out. Now, the eighth volume has been completed and was performed starting last night, it is said.

Star Film Company's "Broken Qin Building" Scheduled to Premiere: The Star Film Company announces that its recently produced film, "Broken Qin Building," was screened for the first time a few days ago. The screenplay was adapted by Zheng Zhengqiu, the narration was written by Mr. Zheng, and the entire film was directed by Mr. Zheng with his full energy. The lead roles are played by Hu Die as Qionghua, Zheng Xiaoqiu as Yunlang, Xia Peizhen as Jiuhuan, and Huang Junfu as Xu Jian. The delicate depictions and rich emotions within are said to be unprecedented in the history of domestic films, making it a major tragedy. To adjust the audience's mood, the company has arranged for Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu, Ms. Hu Die, and others to perform together on stage in a humorous and alluring comedy called "The Test of Love." These two major events are scheduled to premiere at the Central Grand Theater starting March 22nd, it is said.

Business News

New Moon Records' Oil Selling Briskly: The New Moon Record Company, located at 1585 Taoyuan Lane, North Jiangxi Road, announces that since launching its record oil, business has been booming. The company's chemical experts have spent several years painstakingly researching and developing this oil to protect records. Whether using steel or stone needles, any old or worn record, once wiped with this oil, will have its sound brightened and restored to like-new condition, indistinguishable from a newly manufactured record, and it will not deteriorate over time. Major companies and record stores are all selling it, it is said.

Qing Yi Se Restaurant's "He Cai" (Set Meal): Qing Yi Se Restaurant, located at the intersection of Sanma Road and Zhejiang Road, announces that since introducing the six-dish "He Cai" set meal for 1.20 yuan, the restaurant has been even more crowded than before. They have now fully stocked all Cantonese dishes and hired famous chefs to cook them, to serve all enthusiasts, it is said.

Yan Hua Lou Restaurant Adds New Dishes: Yan Hua Lou Restaurant, located across from the Dan Gui First Stage on Sima Road, announces that since the New Year opening, business has been quite prosperous. Recently added dishes include Chicken Oil Spring Bamboo Shoots, Wriggling Oil Spring Bamboo Shoots, and other various seasonal Cantonese dishes, all at reasonable prices and of good quality, it is said.

Beautiful New Arrives with Seasonal Wallpaper: The Beautiful Wallpaper Main Store, located at the Jixian Lane entrance, east of Pentang Lane on Nanjing Road, announces that it has recently shipped in a large batch of spring seasonal art wallpaper and five-color cellophane from Europe and America. There are many styles, about a thousand kinds. If Xianglv hotels, New World Hotels, Guanshengyuan restaurants, Xinglin Hospitals, etc. do not adopt them, the wholesale business in other locations is also very prosperous, it is said.

Pathe Company's Youth Camera: Pathe Company on Sichuan Road announces that its Youth Camera is one of the most ingenious cameras available. It is very easy to shoot with. With one camera in hand, just flip the switch and beautiful scenes can be captured at will. After developing the film at home, it can be shown on the company's Youth Projector. Besides this company, the Pathe Company on Sima Road, the west end of Henan Road, the Lao Bao Fang on Great Horse Road, the Ai Duo Ya Road Zhengjia Mu Bridge Xin Bao Fang also sell it, it is said.

Quan Zuo Trading Company at 2 Jiujiang Road announces that the company has recently added a book and newspaper agency department, specializing in books published by various Shanghai bookstores, as well as daily newspapers, stationery, instruments, etc. The selling price is the same as the bookstores, without charging postage. For the anniversary of its establishment, there is a special discount for one month. All kinds of books are 10% off the actual price, postage is free, and for every dollar spent, a discount coupon of 10 cents will be given, and for every two dollars spent, 100 art letter papers will be given. In addition, the company already has more than 40 national product agency branches, and the business scope has expanded to the Americas. Those who want to serve as a national product branch can contact the company by letter, it is said.

Tong Chang Cloth Store's Market is Lively: Tong Chang Cloth Store on North Stone Road announces that the store's best-selling items daily are domestic fashionable serge, wool flannel, seat fabric, Zhongshan tweed, cheongsam tweed, Star crepe, silk-like flannel, free bamboo, sheet fabric, and the factory's own cloth. Because of their solid materials, they are most suitable for making cotton-padded jackets, with fair prices, it is said.

Efficacy of Minsheng Industrial Society's Ringworm and Scabies Lotion: Minsheng Industrial Society in Yixin Lane, south of the intersection of Nanjing Road and Lloyd Road, announces that its ringworm and scabies lotion specializes in treating various skin ringworm and scabies, as well as Yang Hu Tian Pao and other sores, insect bites that cause itching, and unknown swelling and poisoning, all of which will be cured with just one application. All users praise it enthusiastically. The texture is clean and does not stain clothes. The medicine is of excellent quality and causes no pain, it is said.

Chia Te Red Packet Tonic Pills Selling Well: Ke Fa Pharmacy announces that Chia Te Red Packet Tonic Pills from the United States are purely refined from herbs, and do not contain calomel, mercury, or mineral salts. Its functions are to replenish blood, soothe the liver, and moisten the intestines to promote bowel movements. It can also cure stomach ailments. In China, it has always been managed by Ke Fa Pharmacy, and recently sales have been very prosperous, said to be unprecedented in previous years, it is said.

Desheng Company Changes the Date for Treating Scrofulous Neck: Desheng Gramophone Company at 547 Sima Road announces that, considering that those with scrofulous neck are not only hindered in their ability to have children, but also suffer mental pain, and even face life-threatening dangers. Although patients seek good doctors everywhere, few have been cured, which is a great pity. Therefore, the company has invested in hiring the family-renowned doctor Lu Shunbao, specializing in the treatment of scrofula. Those who need treatment are welcome to seek medical attention. No charge for medicine or fees. However, the originally scheduled dates, which were every third, sixth, and ninth day of the lunar calendar, are now changed to the third, sixth, and ninth Wednesdays of the Gregorian calendar, from 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM. The clinic is located at Guangji Obligatory School in Lane 21, West Street, Xueyuan Road (formerly the old county office) in the city, it is said.
